## Session Handoff — June 17 2026: Summarize UX + Pip orb everywhere + operator goes manual + iOS TTS

**Where things stand:** production (`folioshq.com`) is current through `e3cdd63` on `main` and live. No schema migrations this session — all code-only. The arc, shipped in several pushes:

**iOS TTS (the opening thread).** Pip's voice was totally silent on iOS. Root-caused on-device (persistent debug panel, since removed): Kokoro's `_tts.generate()` **hangs forever on iOS** (82M ONNX model blows the Safari tab-memory cap — no resolve, no throw), so the catch/fallback never ran. Rebuilt the playback path: **WebAudio AudioBuffer built directly from Kokoro's PCM** (no `decodeAudioData`; WebAudio also ignores the Ring/Silent switch, unlike HTMLAudioElement), gesture-time AudioContext unlock + keep-alive, speechSynthesis primed in the gesture, and a **15s timeout on generate → system-voice fallback**. Net: desktop gets the real Kokoro voice; **mobile falls back to the iOS system voice** (Daniel — Chris dislikes it; the real fix is server-side Kokoro, still parked). `src/lib/useKokoroTTS.js`.

**Pip summarize — temperature + the "confusing/complex" UX overhaul.** (1) **Temperature 0.3** on `summary` mode in `api/pip.js` (was API-default ~1.0 — the cause of "great once, nonsense usually"); env-overridable via `PIP_SUMMARY_TEMPERATURE`; threaded as `cfg.temperature` only where a mode opts in. (2) **Scannable rows** — `PipSummarizePreview` rows now render as a one-liner (task text + meta chips: kind · ✦commitment · due · →account) with an **Edit** toggle; the full control stack (assignee/recipient/due/account/project/source) is unchanged but hidden until expanded (`expandedRows` state). Receipts ("What Pip used") collapsed by default. (3) **Pip suggests projects** — the missing half: `SUMMARIZE_SCHEMA_RULES` now emits a shared `suggested_project_title` on ≥2 new_item rows that form one coherent NEW initiative (conservative — most meetings suggest none); `normalizePlanRow` passes it through; the preview groups them into a one-tap "✦ Pip suggests a project — Create & file" banner that creates the Gauge project and routes those rows in via `gaugeProjectId`. (4) **Ad-hoc parity** — `AdHocConversationFlow` now passes `onCreateProject` so one-off conversations get the same project controls as cadence meetings. **VERIFY ON DEVICE:** that suggestion-linked items land where Chris expects in Gauge (folio_tasks.project_id vs stages dual-model — flagged, not yet confirmed).

**Pip orb — new 3D form everywhere (Visual Spec Rule sign-off, in-session).** Cutoff lowered **md→3D** (`md`=32px floor; only the tiny ≤22px `xs`/`sm` inline marks stay classic) — fixes "Pip chat has the old orb" + cards/status banners. Home **hero orb is now clickable → opens Pip chat** (`onOpenPip`). **Speaking ring "zigzag"** added: `PIP_SPEC.speakingRingAmp/Freq/Speed` + optional `speakAmp` arg to `buildPipFrame` (idle passes 0 → byte-identical → **53-test drift lock still passes**); tuned to a subtle tight shimmer (amp 0.03, freq 11, speed 5) after Chris said the first cut "looked like it's dancing." **Floating Pip removed** — bottom-right orb gone on Home (desktop) and on ALL mobile screens (Pip lives in the nav now); **nav-bar Pip lowered** (`marginTop -12→-2`) so it sits in the bar. Both the cutoff + speaking-state changes recorded in the Pip Visual Spec Rule.

**Pip operator — RETIRED THE NIGHTLY CRON, now manual-trigger only.** Per Chris's cost decision (it runs every morning whether or not he opens the app; the report "rarely changes his day"): removed the `crons` entry from `vercel.json`. `api/operator-run.js` now accepts **either** the cron secret (privileged) **or a valid Supabase user JWT** (scopes the run strictly to that user — the browser button can't hold the cron secret). New `OperatorRunButton` on Home (`src/views/home/OperatorRunButton.jsx`): authenticates with the user's session token, ~20-40s working state, refetches the report on completion; renders as a prompt card when there's no report today, a subtle "↻ Refresh" when there is. **Knowledge is unaffected** — the operator pass *reads* memory, doesn't write it; daily health snapshots are written on app-open, not by the pass. Brief auto-advance bug fixed in the same arc: the Start-My-Day brief advances on `speaking` true→false, but the system-voice fallback never set `speaking=true`, so it froze on "Your word" — new `fallbackSpeak()` drives the state, and Kokoro is marked failed-for-session after one timeout so later cards skip the 15s wait.

**"Is Folios earning its keep?" — new read-only dashboard** (top of Settings → Pip). `useFolioHealth` reads `folio_pip_usage` + `pip_correction_log` + `folio_meetings` (account stats from accounts in memory) → feed-rate (days fed / accounts touched-vs-cold), accuracy (corrections last 14d + trend + top type), a canary (flags the operator run if silent ≥3d), cost (30d + top spender + week-over-week), and a deterministic one-line verdict. No new tables, no writes, no Pip calls; fails soft to "—".

**Open follow-ups:** (1) **server-side Pip voice** — the only fix for the good voice on mobile + the first-card 15s wait (parked, recommended next). (2) **Docs still call the operator a nightly cron** — `docs/` suite + a few in-file references need squaring to "manual trigger"; not done this session. (3) device-tune pass: nav Pip position, md-orb muddiness, zigzag amplitude, summarize temp/suggestion frequency. (4) the Home "draft-ahead" card email question (is that the auto-email Chris flagged?) still unanswered. (5) a true accept-vs-edit accuracy metric would need logging accepted rows.



**Where things stand:** production (`folioshq.com`) is current through commit `ec71b25` on `main` and live. No schema migrations this session — all changes are code-only. Two docs updates pending (PDFs not regenerated this session; no capability-level docs changed).

Follow-ups inserted as `source:'followup'`, `priority:10` so they float to the top of the drip queue immediately. No chaining (follow-up to a follow-up is suppressed; terminology questions never get follow-ups). Hook's internal `fetch` callback renamed → `loadRows` to avoid shadowing global `fetch` API. Queue query updated to `.in("source", ["gap_observed", "followup"])`.
- **Item 37 (org structure reasoning):** `api/generate-questions.js` now splits accounts into two labeled blocks before sending to Sonnet — "YOUR OWN INTERNAL TEAMS / DEPARTMENTS (you ARE part of these — NOT external relationships)" and "YOUR MANAGED ACCOUNTS (external suppliers, partners, clients)". Added ORG STRUCTURE system-prompt rule. Pip now knows not to ask "who owns MSO relationships?" when a dept called "MSO Team" exists.
- **Item 38 (ownership distinction):** `api/operator-run.js` — added `owner_user_id` to the accounts select; `renderAccountContext` emits `RELATIONSHIP_OWNER: NO` for accounts where `owner_user_id !== userId`; `ACCOUNT_SYSTEM` prompt rule instructs Pip to suppress outreach/follow-up/cold-nudge suggestions for such accounts and only surface project-level work. `HomeView.jsx` — `coldAccounts` filter and `anomalySignals` forEach both skip accounts not owned by userId. MSO accounts (set to "Not mine" via the header toggle) now vanish from cold-contact nudges and anomaly signals on Home.
- **Item 48 partial (spend cap wired into operator-run):** `overDailySpendCap(admin, userId)` is now called in `gatherAndRun` after `pickMovedAccounts`; if over cap, `moved` is set to `[]` (deep passes all skipped, roll-up still runs on prior state). Uses the service-role admin client with explicit `user_id` filter — correct under RLS bypass. Cost constants in `_pipUsage.js` were ALREADY correct (haiku: in:0.1/out:0.5, sonnet: in:0.3/out:1.5) — the CLAUDE.md "1000× wrong" complaint was stale from a prior session that already fixed it.

**No migrations pending. `scripts/test-api-imports.js` updated** to include `api/followup-question.js` (now 12 handlers in the array).

**Also shipped this session — dropdown uniformity + Pip people context audit (commit `a40c9b9`):**
- **Full person-picker audit.** Conducted a codebase-wide audit of every person-selection field, name vs. email display surface, and Pip context gap. 13 fixes shipped in one batch.
- **PersonPicker default storage fix** — contacts were stored as `c.email || c.name` by default, meaning any contact with an email address would be stored/displayed as their email. Changed default to `c.name`. Every caller that needs email-based storage already explicitly overrides this, so no regressions. Root cause of "email showing instead of name" in most surfaces.
- **AddUpdateModal Owner** — replaced the hand-rolled custom typeahead with the shared `PersonPicker` (account contacts → My Team → free-text). `contacts` prop threaded through `UpdatesTab` → `AccountDetail`.
- **ProjectModal Requested By + External Contact** — both replaced with `PersonPicker`. External Contact keeps `external_contact_id` in sync when a known contact name is selected.
- **ScheduleMeetingModal multi-account + attendees** — two features in one: (1) account picker now supports **multiple accounts** (chips, removable; `account_ids[]` in payload, primary `account_id` = first selected); (2) after account selection, the primary account's contacts appear as **attendee toggle buttons** so you can tag who the meeting is with at schedule time. `contacts={allContacts}` threaded from App.jsx.
- **resolveAssignee display fix** (`StandingBoardView`, `FlatTaskQueue`) — removed `email.split("@")[0]` fallback that was leaking raw email local-parts onto kanban cards and queue rows.
- **Pip context: project + task people** — `pipContext.js` now includes `assignee` and `requested_by` on each active project line; task-level `assignee_email` and `recipient` surfaced under each project's tasks. Pip can now say "Dana owns the All Star rebuild" in briefs.
- **Pip context: owner normalization** — `normalizePerson()` helper converts raw email strings to readable names before Pip reads open-item owners, update owners, and project/task assignees.
- **Pip unknown-person detection hardened** (`pip.js`) — prompt now requires cross-referencing the full CONTACTS list (exact and first-name matches) before flagging anyone as unknown. Internal/department meetings (`internal_team` account type) always return an empty `unknown_people` list — Pip will no longer suggest adding your own colleagues as new contacts.
- **Schema** — `folio_meetings.account_ids uuid[] DEFAULT '{}'` applied to prod via MCP migration + folded into `schema.sql`.

## 🎯 GAME PLAN — DRAFT (June 10 2026 — awaiting Chris's teardown; ALL BUILDS PAUSED until he approves)

Built from the audit + the interview. Organizing principle is Chris's own arc: **Phase 0 harden → Phase 1 safety (nothing dropped, never flat-footed) → Phase 2 shine (promotion-visible).** Every item must respect the Pip Data Line Rule + App Coherence Rule.

### Phase 0 — Hardening — ✅ SHIPPED June 10 2026 PM (commits 13fb1f5 + 2fb097b + d246256 on main)

All items below are DONE except three deliberately rejected on sanity-pass: fetchAllContacts/fetchAllUpdates relocation (Home brief + gap detection + schedule modal consume them at startup), computeAndSaveSnapshots in-memory reuse (needs unlimited narrow-column meetings; in-memory copy is now capped at 300), and the org-layered "duplicate" policies on folio_accounts/folio_org_members/folio_tasks (intentional own+org access, kept). DB migrations applied to prod via MCP (rls_initplan_wrap_folio_tables, drop_duplicate_quick_tasks_policy, fk_indexes_folio_tables) + schema.sql synced. Index chunk 670→194 kB. CI now runs npm run test (195 tests, 3 new suites: accountHealth, lifeLadder, pipPlanApply). Build process used: Sonnet Patch executed the mechanical spec in a worktree (no push), main session reviewed line-by-line, fixed one docs-heading clobber, layered the structural items, shipped.
- **Bugs:** `api/ask-pip.js` raw-JSON-on-truncation (copy portfolio-brief's regex-salvage + check `stop_reason`); `api/operator-run.js` silent empty operator state on JSON parse failure (log raw output to console/`folio_errors`); un-suppress commitment nudges when operator report active (`HomeView.jsx` ~line 1236); dead "Open brief →" pill when no calls today (~line 1020); ISO date leaking into draft-ahead card.
- **Safety nets:** add `npm run test` to `.github/workflows/ci.yml`; write tests for `accountHealth.js` + `pipPlanApply.js` (+ `lifeLadder.js` later); register `api/invite.js` in `scripts/test-api-imports.js`; attach JWT to `profile-synthesis.js` client (latent footgun).
- **API guards:** server rate-limit on `portfolio-brief.js`; `export const config = { maxDuration: 60 }` on `portfolio-brief.js` + `business-review.js`; truncation detection in `leadership-readout.js`; `generate-questions.js` model failures → 500 (not 200-with-modelError).
- **Performance:** lazy-load `AccountDetail` + `StartConversationModal` + `AddAccountModal` + `PipCatchUp` (cuts ~150–200 kB off the 670 kB index chunk); dynamic-import `pip.js` out of App.jsx (only `compressCorrectionsPip` used); `.limit()` on global `useMeetings` + size-guard its localStorage cache; fix `CadenceMeetingMode` ESC-handler re-registration on every keystroke (useRef); reduce cold-open queries ~27→~15 (move `fetchAllContacts`/`fetchAllUpdates` into AccountDetail; collapse drip-question triple query; pass in-memory data to `computeAndSaveSnapshots`).
- **DB (apply via MCP + fold into schema.sql):** wrap RLS `auth.uid()` in `(select auth.uid())` (76 lints); consolidate duplicate permissive policies (90 lints, worst: `folio_quick_tasks`, `folio_accounts`); add missing FK indexes / drop unused ones.
- **Cheap Pip parity wins (from audit):** wire `recentUpdates` (update calendar) into summarize payload; inject operator state (`operator_situation`/`risks`/`headline`) into chat context; add `relationship_role` to Brief Me contacts; add `status_updates` pulse to generate-questions' project query.
- **Docs catch-up:** June 10 features into `product-overview.md` + `upgrades.md`, regenerate PDFs (standing rule currently violated).
- **Theme-token sweep:** worst offenders (`ProjectsTab.jsx` status map, `SettingsView` `#fff`, `AddAccountModal`, `AuthView`).

### Phase 1 — SAFETY (the keeper of his word)

2. **Team request queue in Folios — Folios is the MASTER, the Excel is an OUTPUT.** *(✅ BUILT June 21 2026 as the "Team Sheet" — branch `claude/folios-onboarding-th7bv5`, NOT shipped; see the June-21 handoff at the top. He then **exports changed rows as tab-separated lines in the sheet's exact column order** (pastes straight into Excel cells) for the team/admin who work off the sheet. Folios **tracks dirty rows since last export and reminds him** — timing-aware (Mon afternoon / Tue morning, before the team meeting): "4 updates aren't on the team sheet yet — copy them?" One tap copies exactly those lines. This fixes the thing Chris says he's currently bad at (keeping the sheet updated) and kills the two-system drift without requiring the admin or boss to change behavior. Plus a clean meeting-ready view he can screen-share Tuesdays.
3. **Win log / brag file + commitment integrity stats** — *(✅ BUILT June 21 2026 — branch `claude/folios-onboarding-th7bv5`, NOT shipped; batched with #4. `folio_wins` table + `useWins` + Win log in Settings → Pip + "Promises kept" stat. 5. **Portable-brain depth:** semantic search over all notes/summaries (pgvector); "since you were here" per-account deltas (operator delta + per-device last-open already exist); meeting-aware timing (prep surfaces auto-raised ~15 min before calls; first real use of PWA push).
6. **Instruction-writer for the admin** (work-Claude side owns file analysis; Pip drafts the crayon-level instruction docs from account/project context; track handoff status in the waiting-on layer).

### Success criteria (~3 months out — check these, don't vibe them)
1. Chris opens Folios at 9am and in <60s knows what he owes, what's today, and has answered Pip's ≤3 check-in questions — and the corrected report is accurate.
2. No flat-footed Mondays — the 1:1 pack means nothing the boss raises is a surprise.
3. Most meeting summaries apply with zero cleanup; task counts are small and right.
4. The email/Teams day reaches Folios daily via the digest, and it shows — account pages worth opening, chat worth asking.
5. Chris never maintains the same information in two places by hand — the team sheet is generated from Folios (export + reminder loop); the drift problem is dead.

If any criterion stays false, that's where we dig next — design failure, not user failure (especially #4: if the digest habit doesn't stick in 3 weeks, redesign the friction, don't blame the habit).

**51. Pip intelligence roadmap (TIER 1 — accuracy/trust; see consolidated tier map above) — "feed Pip more reality before making it a better thinker" (QUEUED June 24 2026, from a 3-round Claude↔ChatGPT design exchange Chris ran)** — *(NOT built — captured so it doesn't die in chat. Chris bounced "how does Pip work / how to improve him" off ChatGPT across 3 rounds; the two AIs converged hard. This is the distilled, de-duped roadmap + the decisions already locked. Build order is MINE (Claude's) recommendation, greenlit-pending. NOTE post-consolidation: 1b "end-of-day brain dump" now lives under item 52(A) as the canonical capture-inbox home — it's a scheduled trigger on that inbox, not a separate build.)* The unifying insight (the one I'd weight above everything): **the binding constraint is the CAPTURE GAP — Pip only sees ~10% of Chris's day — so reasoning upgrades have a ceiling until more reality is in. Prioritize capture at least as highly as smarter reasoning.** The bundle, in recommended order:
   - **(1a) Explainable health** — never just "At Risk"; always "At Risk *because* — no substantive touch 24d · supplier owes May follow-up · implementation project inactive." **We already COMPUTE these signals in `gatherSignals` (accountHealth.js) and throw them away** — this is surfacing existing data, near-zero effort, biggest trust win per hour. Account health pill caption + Pip's health language both read the reasons. **Effort S.**
   - **(1b) End-of-day brain dump** — a 4:30pm nudge: "Anything happen today that isn't in here?" → free-text → Pip structures + files it. **Reuses `QuickCaptureModal` + `api/parse-digest` wholesale** (it's quick-capture on a daily trigger with multi-row parse). Highest capture-gap recovery per minute; cheap. **Effort S.** *(1a + 1b are the bundle I'd ship FIRST — small, compounding, touch nothing risky.)*
   - **(2a) Counter-evidence before any "stalled/dropped" alarm** — before Pip cries fire, it must search for evidence AGAINST the alarm (recent note / digest mention / related project moved) and downgrade confidence if found. **This IS the All Star Monday bug** ("work done over the weekend, just unmarked; Pip screamed overdue-fire"). Uses retrieval we already have (semantic recall + `search_notes`). Complements the existing personal-baseline anomaly check + the two-way morning check-in. **Effort M.**
   - **(2b) Ownership inference from notes** — auto-extract "waiting on John since [date]" from *"John said he'd get back next week"* at summarize time, instead of manual `waiting_on` flags. The real "who has the ball" upgrade. **DECISION LOCKED: evidence-backed, NO decay-math / NO fabricated confidence %** (both AIs agreed 0.82→0.35 is invented precision that fights the staleness-humility work). Surface it as evidence + elapsed-time ("waiting on John · he said next week · 18d, no mention since"), which is what the aged board already does honestly. **Effort M.**
   - **(3) Commitment confidence buckets in summarize** — classify extracted lines as explicit commitment / likely / discussion-point so "we talked about reporting" never becomes a task. Prompt-level sharpening of the precision-over-volume doctrine + existing `is_commitment` flag. **Effort S** (watch it doesn't just add UI noise).
   - **(4) Soft-structured digest (handoff format upgrade)** — keep the digest paste FREE-FORM (the #49 de-brand explicitly rejected rigid `[OWE]/[WAITING]` tags — do not regress that), but make work-Claude's prose follow a *predictable shape* and make Pip's EXTRACTION richer: pull sentiment / stakeholder-changes / momentum / risk, not just owe/waiting/touch. Richer output schema, NOT a stiffer input contract. **Effort M.**
   - **(5) Relationship facts — EVIDENCE-ONLY, computed-over-inferred** — store only traceable facts: recurring-theme counts ("onboarding raised 4×"), commitment history (made/kept-on-time/missed — **this is a COUNT from the promise log, not a judgment**), role evolution. **DECISION LOCKED: do NOT persist soft traits** (trust/influence/communication-style) — both AIs agreed an inferred "Mike is unreliable" becomes a lens that compounds bias. **Effort L.**
   - **(6) Account Narrative Memory — the high-ceiling / high-risk one, build LAST** — a persisted "story of the relationship" (began at integration → strong early → slowed on resource constraints → renewed interest → hinges on onboarding). Maps onto Chris's core need ("I can't problem-solve unless I know the account cold"). **CRITICAL DESIGN DECISION (mine, neither AI caught it): build it RE-DERIVED, not ACCUMULATING.** An accreting narrative has the EXACT bias-lock failure ChatGPT itself flagged for traits, one level up — a wrong "supplier is resource-constrained" becomes a lens over the whole account. So: re-derive the arc from evidence on each material change (the F3 event-driven pattern, extended to a longitudinal read), keep `folio_account_snapshots` as the evidence floor so it can always be rebuilt vs. blindly trusted, and **extend the existing account-state read rather than add a parallel narrative table** (App Coherence — no second drifting store). **Effort L.** Earns its spot last, after the cheap accuracy/capture wins prove out.
   - **REJECTED (don't resurrect):** clipboard watcher (compliance landmine — slurps raw corporate email/numbers; also browser clipboard needs a paste gesture; manual paste already exists); fabricated confidence percentages anywhere (fights staleness-humility); rigid-tag digest template (regresses #49). **VALIDATED current architecture:** event-driven account state + meeting-specific retrieval is right — do NOT build a giant always-on full-history context (token explosion + stale reasoning).

**52. The Mastermind / Synthesis layer — Pip connects the dots across the fire hose (QUEUED June 24 2026, Chris's vision — the PAYOFF that makes the capture habit worth it)** — *(NOT built — captured + being designed with Chris. This is the thesis that ties item 51 together: now that Chris is feeding daily email digests + stray captures, he wants Pip to SYNTHESIZE the stream over time, not just file rows. His words: "if I give him 3 days in a row of 'Tara at LKQ is going to give me account numbers for X shops,' I want him to realize I keep bringing this up and offer to DO something — build a Gauge project? chase it? — that's the level of thinking I want. He should scan all this and piece things together." + "what if I had ONE spot to shove info in and Pip becomes a mastermind that sees it all and makes suggestions.")*
   - **⭐ NORTH STAR (the FEELING, not the mechanics — Chris, June 24 2026, articulating the bar he can't fully spec):** "I want it to seriously feel like Pip is a genius reading everything and feeding it into each account… Pip should basically be me in there… someone should be blown away by what Pip can produce." What he's actually describing is an EXPERIENCE, not a feature — decoded into three layers, in BUILD ORDER (this ordering is the strategy, not just a list): **(1) The river reaches every faucet** — everything Chris dumps must SATURATE each account's context, so the cadence brief / pre-call brief / account state already KNOW what he fed Pip in his summaries. The pipes exist (F1 shared `buildAccountContext`, F2 persisted, F3 event-driven recompute, F6 recall) — the work is making the capture stream actually flow through them richly (relationship texture + momentum + "what we talked about last time," not just filed tasks). This is the FOUNDATION; the suggestions are a bolt-on without it. **(2) The instant pre-call brief is the "blown-away" moment** — Chris's own example ("jumping on a call, need a brief quick → last time they emailed you talked about X"). Tap one button → *where you stand · last contact you discussed X · you owe Y · they've gone quiet on Z · the one thing to raise is W.* Specific, grounded in his own words, ~10s. This single surface, done well, IS the "someone's blown away" demo — it's not a dashboard, it's Pip handing him his own brain back, caught up, on demand. **(3) THEN the proactive mastermind suggestions** (the A/B halves below). **WHY THIS ORDER = the answer to "I don't want the first proposal to be WTF":** grounded surfaces (briefs that QUOTE his reality back) literally CAN'T produce a WTF — they're not guessing, they're reciting what he said. Start there, earn trust that Pip reads the room correctly, and ONLY THEN do the bolder "you keep mentioning Tara — make a project?" suggestions land as genius instead of noise. You earn "genius" by starting grounded, not by starting big. If only the pre-call brief shipped well, the north-star feeling is already mostly delivered; the mastermind is the encore, not the opening act.
   - **(A) One capture inbox — "shove anything in here."** Elevate quick-capture into THE always-available brain-dump: the daily email digest AND stray one-liners ("just spoke with Dan, he's getting me a new file to upload") go to the same place. Every line is filed by kind (task/waiting/touch) AND retained as a lightweight signal the synthesis pass reasons over. Reuses `QuickCaptureModal` + `api/parse-digest`. Answer to Chris's "should I throw info in even if it's not on the summary?" → **YES, that's the whole point** — the more reality in, the smarter the synthesis (item 51's capture-gap thesis).
   - **(B) The synthesis pass — the actual "mastermind."** A periodic (daily / event-gated, NOT always-on) Sonnet pass over recent stream items (tasks, captures, digest rows, waiting-ons, recent notes) that detects **recurrence + convergence + stalls** and emits a SMALL set of high-confidence proactive suggestions. The four patterns worth surfacing: (1) **same pending thing mentioned N days running** (Tara/account-numbers ×3) → "you keep raising this — promote to a Gauge project? chase it? it's been open 6d"; (2) **a promise that recurs but never closes** = a stall signal → chase/escalate; (3) **convergent theme across accounts** ("file upload" with Dan AND Tara → maybe a process problem, not two account problems); (4) **a waiting-on that's gone quiet past the account's own rhythm**. Pip PROPOSES, Chris approves (one-tap → creates the project / chase note / waiting-on). 
   - **CAPABILITY MENU — the "level of ability" Chris wants (June 24 2026 — these are illustrations of the BAR, not a build list; the assignee example in item 54 was just one of many). The unifying mechanism in every one: stream + memory → a SPECIFIC, GROUNDED move Chris didn't ask for. Clerk → chief of staff.** Grouped by type of thinking:
     - **Connect threads across time/accounts:** "3 suppliers flagged the same product-team delay this week — that's one product problem, not three account problems; draft a boss summary?" · "'onboarding friction' has hit LKQ 4× in 6 weeks and never resolved — it's becoming the thing the account hinges on." · "two stalled projects both wait on the same product person — one conversation unblocks both."
     - **Walk into every call caught up (pre-call brief, full form):** "call with Tara in 20 min — last email you owed her the shop file, doesn't look sent; top of your brief." · "LKQ Thursday — last two meetings you gave timelines that slipped, they'll ask; here's where it really stands."
     - **Catch what falls through:** "you told Dan 'this week,' it's Thursday, no note it went out — did it?" · "Adam's quiet on the macro 9d, usually 3 — chase?" · reading a summary: "new name Sarah at LKQ, not in contacts, sounds like a decision-maker — add her?"
     - **Read between the lines of his own notes:** "last two All Star notes read tenser ('still waiting,' 'frustrated') — flag cooling?" · "the way you described LKQ, sounds like expansion talk — bump tier/cadence?"
     - **Produce the artifact, not just the reminder:** "here's a chase email to LKQ's POC + an internal product nudge, both drafted off what you fed me." · "Monday pack ready: promised-vs-done, what moved, what's stuck + why." · "turn this week's LKQ notes into a team-sheet row?"
     - **Manage HIM, not just accounts (capacity/triage):** "6 commitments due this week, 3 same day — 2 can slip unnoticed, 1 angers a supplier; do them in this order." · "4 new commitments in today's summaries — heavy day; most time-sensitive is the All Star audit."
     - **Root cause under the symptoms (highest wow, build last):** "LKQ's last 4 asks all point at one need — reporting; you've solved them one-off; propose ONE project that fixes the root?"
     - **REACHABILITY MAP:** CLOSEST (bones exist, just need the stream flowing in) = pre-call brief · dropped-commitment catch · chase-email drafts · Monday pack · recall-on-demand. MIDDLE (new synthesis on data we hold) = cross-account thread-connect · tone/momentum from prose · capacity triage. FURTHEST (genuine strategist, earn trust first) = root-cause spotting · "product problem not account problem." **Across ALL of it the one rule holds: Pip proposes, Chris approves, speaks ONLY when it genuinely has something — the 10-mediocre-observations-a-day version is worse than nothing.**
   - **ROUND-4 REFINEMENTS (June 24 2026 — 2nd Claude↔ChatGPT exchange + Chris "I want Pip to be a better version of me, not just follow what I do"; Claude vetted, these are KEEPERS):**
     - **🔒 THE 4-PART INSIGHT GATE (lock this for the whole mastermind layer):** every proactive observation MUST answer all four — (1) Evidence (what happened), (2) Why it matters (why Chris should care), (3) Proposed action, (4) Expected outcome. **If Pip can't fill all four → it says NOTHING.** This is the concrete enforcement of precision-over-volume — not a vibe, a gate.
     - **QUARANTINE bold reframes OUT of operational surfaces.** The pre-call brief / daily brief / waiting board stay GROUNDED + reliable; strategic reframes live in their OWN surface ("Pip's Observations" — = the item-52 "connected some dots" card, max 1-2, not necessarily daily). **The line: FACTS flow everywhere (waiting-ons, themes-as-data into account context); OPINIONS/reframes stay quarantined** so a wrong strategic take never poisons the brief Chris depends on daily.
     - **OPPORTUNITY-COST prioritization** ("if you do ONE thing today, do this — it touches 3 projects + a relationship at risk"). Underweighted vs pattern-detection; best AMs out-prioritize, not out-remember. CAVEAT: rank on CONCRETE signals (deadline, # stakeholders affected, stall age) — never Pip's gut, or a confidently-wrong "do this first" beats a plain list.
     - **🔒 FEATURE-SELECTION TEST (lock it):** "Does this make Pip more ACCURATE about reality, or more USEFUL at changing Chris's decisions? If neither → it's noise disguised as intelligence." The filter that prevents building a very intelligent OBSERVER (trivia) instead of a chief of staff (changes decisions).
     - **⭐ DECISION JOURNAL — the real mechanism for "me, but better" (the best new idea; build LATE = Level 3, after the foundation).** Quietly log the CALLS Chris makes (promoted X to a project · escalated Y · bumped Z's cadence) + the why + the outcome, so later Pip can say *"last few times something recurred like this you made it a project and it moved — do that here?"* Why it's the ONLY true answer to "better than me": a generic "better" (imported best-practice) IS the wtf Chris wants to avoid; "better" only works grounded in HIS OWN track record. Build rules: **INFER decisions from the action he already took (don't interrogate / no forms); HUMBLE on outcomes (correlation, not "works 80%" — same no-fabricated-confidence rule); LATE (assumes the grounded layer works).** Likely its own queue item when it's time. The LADDER: L1 remember for me → L2 think like me → L3 improve me; earn each before the next (and note: item 55 proves L1 is currently leaking, so foundation-first).
   - **WHAT WE ALREADY HAVE to build on (don't reinvent):** `useRecentThemes` (cross-account theme detection, already feeds the daily brief), the `waiting_on`/aged-board layer, semantic recall (F6) + `search_notes`, the operator-pass pattern (this is the operator pass pointed at the capture STREAM instead of account-by-account), drip/follow-up questions (the proactive-nudge surface already exists). Mostly a NEW synthesis prompt + a recurrence query over existing rows + a suggestions surface — not a new data store (App Coherence: the tasks/captures already ARE the stream; don't add a parallel "stream" table).
   - **THE TWO THINGS THAT MAKE OR BREAK IT (my flags as the honest coworker):** (1) **PRECISION OVER VOLUME or it dies.** Chris's #1 Pip allergy is task/suggestion explosion. A mastermind that suggests a project every time something repeats twice = noise = trust death. HARD threshold + real confidence + "no suggestion is a valid output"; recurrence ≠ importance (something said 3× may just be him thinking out loud — Pip must tell "recurring because stuck/important" from "recurring because chatty"). Start with ONE suggestion/day max, earn the right to more. (2) **DATA LINE pressure goes UP with the fire hose.** "Account numbers for X shops" is literally shop identifiers + counts = on the data line. The retained signals + any synthesis output must GENERALIZE ("supplier sending shop account data" not the numbers/list). More raw corporate text flowing in = more chances for numbers to lodge in Pip-authored memory — the generalization guards must be tight on the capture-parse AND the synthesis pass.
   - **HOW IT STAYS CHEAP + non-stale (the architecture answer to "see it all"):** NOT a giant always-on context (rejected in item 51). A focused periodic synthesis query over a bounded recent window (last ~7–14d of stream items, titles/themes only), one Sonnet call, cached + fingerprint-gated like the operator pass + Monday pack — re-runs only when the stream actually moved. Suggestions persist until acted on/dismissed.
   - **OPEN DESIGN Qs for Chris:** where the suggestions surface (Home "Pip connected some dots ✦" card? a dedicated synthesis view? inside the daily brief?); cadence (daily, or live as he dumps?); how aggressive (1/day vs. surface-everything-confident); does a promoted suggestion create a Gauge project directly or a draft for him to flesh out. **Depends on item 51's (1b) capture inbox + recurring-theme groundwork — build that first, then this is the capstone.**
   - **RESOLVED DESIGN — account pin on the dump box (June 24 2026):** the capture inbox gets an OPTIONAL top-level "pin this dump to [account]" dropdown that acts as a **default, NOT a lock**. (a) Single-account brain-dump: pin it → every extracted row with no account of its own lands there (no repeating the name). (b) Email summary across many accounts: leave it blank → Pip routes each row per-line as today. **Rule: per-row account detection ALWAYS overrides the pin** (a line that names its own account wins), so a stray pin can't hijack a multi-account paste. The per-row editable AccountPicker in the review step (already in `QuickCaptureModal`) is the safety net regardless — nothing files until confirmed. DO NOT make the pin force ALL rows to one account (that would wreck a multi-account paste). Rule of thumb for Chris: one account on his mind → pin; pasting the daily summary → leave blank.

**53. Desktop autocorrect — iPhone-style auto-replace in prose fields (QUEUED June 24 2026, Chris "side thing")** — *(NOT built. Chris wants obvious typos + contractions fixed as he types — "arent" → "aren't", "teh" → "the" — like an iPhone keyboard.)* KEY FACT: on his iPhone the OS keyboard ALREADY autocorrects any text field; the gap is **desktop** (browsers give the red squiggly `spellcheck` underline but do NOT auto-replace). He's 90% desktop, so the payoff is a built-in layer. **Recommended approach (the sweet spot — NOT a full dictionary):** a curated high-confidence replacement map — contractions (arent/dont/wont/cant/im/ive/youre/theyre/didnt/doesnt/isnt/wasnt/werent/hasnt/havent/wouldnt/couldnt/shouldnt…) + the few-hundred most-common English typos (teh→the, recieve→receive, seperate→separate, definately→definitely…). Fire ONLY on a completed word (space/enter/punctuation), replace in place, leave a one-step undo (Ctrl+Z already works on a textarea edit; optionally backspace-reverts like iOS). **THE ONE GOTCHA that makes or breaks it — protect proper nouns / jargon / account names.** Must NOT "correct" Fuse5, MSO, LKQ, account/contact names, or anything capitalized mid-typing — those are exactly the words a dumb autocorrect mangles. So: skip capitalized words, skip anything matching the glossary (`folio_pip_facts`) or an account/contact name, keep the map curated (no fuzzy full-dictionary matching → no false positives on names). **Scope:** the big free-text PROSE surfaces only — meeting notes editor, quick-capture, note textareas — NOT every input (never autocorrect an email/account-name/due-date field). **Coherence:** lives as ONE shared helper (`src/lib/autocorrect.js`) and plugs into the SAME textareas as `useAutoBullet` (which already does sentence auto-capitalization) — don't reimplement per surface. **Data-line nuance:** this is a TYPING AID happening visibly as he types (like the keyboard), with undo — NOT Pip silently editing saved notes, so it doesn't violate "Pip never silently edits user text" (different thing: a keyboard feature, reversible, user sees it). Deterministic, zero AI cost. **Effort S.** Quick partial win to check first: confirm no prose textarea sets `autoCorrect="off"`/`spellCheck={false}` (that would suppress even the iOS keyboard's native autocorrect on mobile).

**54. Pip learns your HABITS → offers to codify them (QUEUED June 24 2026, Chris — the second axis of "wow")** — *(NOT built. Chris: "does he have the ability to do things like 'I've noticed you always assign Adam for X task. Want me to hard-code him as the owner of this type of task?'" A DIFFERENT axis from item 52: 52 = patterns in the WORK/RELATIONSHIPS (Tara/projects); THIS = patterns in HOW CHRIS OPERATES (his own workflow habits) → offer to automate them. Both are "wow," complementary.)* The category: **operational pattern learning → proposed defaults/automations.** Pip watches how Chris repeatedly does things and OFFERS to codify each as a reversible default. Examples: "you've assigned Adam the last 4 integration tasks — make him the default owner for those?" · "you always set audits ~2 weeks out — pre-fill that due date?" · "every LKQ meeting you create a follow-up — auto-suggest it next time?" · "you keep re-tagging these as commitments — flag this type automatically?"
   - **⚡ HALF-BUILT ALREADY — `pip_assignment_hints` is the engine for the Adam example.** Pip ALREADY learns assignee patterns: `pip_assignment_hints (account_id, task_pattern, assignee_email)` is written when Chris overrides an assignee in the summarize preview, fed back into the next summarize, AND promoted to a cross-account hint (`account_id=null`) once ≥3 distinct account-specific hints share the same `task_pattern`+`assignee`. **The gap is it's SILENT** — it learns + auto-applies without ever surfacing "I noticed this, want to lock it in?" or showing a receipt when a learned default fires. This item = give that silent learning a VISIBLE, CONSENT-BASED voice (+ extend the same pattern-detect→offer shape to due-dates, follow-ups, commitment-tagging, routing).
   - **THE MAGIC DETAIL = RECEIPTS.** When a learned default fires, Pip shows its work: "I set Adam as owner here — you usually do. (undo)". That visible feedback is the "Pip is alive / it's learning me" moment Chris has wanted for a while (the receipts theme) AND doubles as proof the capture habit is paying off.
   - **THE TWO RULES (same as everything — break them and it's annoyance, not wow):** (1) **PROPOSE, never silently impose** — always offers ("want me to lock this in?"), Chris taps yes, everything codified is REVERSIBLE; he's never surprised by Pip having changed how things work. (NB: the current `pip_assignment_hints` auto-applies silently — this item should add the offer + receipt so it stops being a black box.) (2) **HIGH BAR** — only offer after a REAL pattern (~4 consistent instances), never after 2; recurrence ≠ a rule. A stream of "want me to automate this?" prompts is task-explosion in a nicer hat — one good offer beats ten eager ones; "no offer" is the default state.
   - **DATA LINE:** assignee/due-date/routing/tagging patterns are workflow metadata, not business numbers — safe. (Don't let a learned "default" ever encode a customer count / shop list / number.)
   - **WHY IT MATTERS:** the difference between an assistant that REMEMBERS and one that ANTICIPATES — "I know how you'd do this, want me to just do it?" That's the chief-of-staff feeling, and the assignee half already has its engine. **Surface it where the work happens** (summarize preview, task create, the proposed-default offer as a drip-style card) — reuse the existing offer/receipt surfaces, don't add a parallel one (App Coherence). **Build relationship to 52:** these are the two faces of "Pip's proactive intelligence" — 52 reasons over content, 54 reasons over Chris's behavior; ship 52's grounded foundation first (north star), then 54 rides the same propose-and-approve plumbing.

**44. Pip 3D redesign — "Bold Hex" (DESIGN LOCKED by Chris, June 10 2026 — do not alter without his explicit say-so)** — Chris approved the **Bold Hex** variant from the v4 mockup (`mockups/pip-hex-ring-final.html`, branch `claude/magical-bohr-ex126v` — that file is visual ground truth). The design: Pip's two spheres (current proportions, head bright / tail 0.42) re-skinned as **hex-tiled lattices over a soft glowing core**, floating inside a **hex-tiled torus ring** with an organic drifting twist (not a perfect circle — "no tire"), diagonally tilted, visibly spinning. **ONE breath clock (4.8s — slowed from 2.4 on June 10 2026, the breath was the perceived-speed problem; classic small orbs keep the 2.4s CSS breathe) drives every hexagon in the figure** — ring cells + sphere cells open/close together (`bs = 0.55+0.56·breath`), ring swells, core glow brightens, all in sync.
   - **FROZEN PARAMETERS** (from the mockup's Bold Hex cfg; changing ANY of these = changing Pip = requires Chris): ring `R 84, rt 18, nu 16, nv 4, tiltX 0.40, tiltY −0.48, spin 0.18 rad/s (slowed from 0.45 by Chris, June 10 2026 — too fast at full size), sw 1.6, warp 16, wob 6, fill:false, motionScale 1.0 (knob scales ALL rotation+twist time, never breath; tried 0.4 then reverted — the fast motion was the breath)`; ring swell `R×(0.97+0.05·breath)`, tube `rt×(0.92+0.12·breath)`; radius waver `1+0.055·sin(2u−0.33t)`, twist `warp·sin(2u+0.9−0.41t)+wob·sin(3u+0.27t)`; spheres head `r16 @ (0,−16), n=18 hexes, spin 0.3`, tail `r11.2 @ (0,18), n=10, spin −0.26, opacity 0.42`; hex size `1.9/√n`; perspective `FP 480 / FS 5`; 4 depth buckets at z ±0.4 with opacities `.16/.34/.66/.95` and stroke widths `×0.8/0.9/1.05/1.25`; sphere-group breathe `scale 1+0.08·breath`; colors ONLY from accent tokens (accent / hi / deep) so Life-mode dusty-orange reskins automatically.
   - **Lock-down plan (the "Pip never drifts again" guarantee), to build on ship:** (1) single canonical `PipOrb3D` component, spec as a frozen `PIP_SPEC` constant block — every surface renders through it, nothing redraws Pip inline; (2) **deterministic geometry unit test** — render one frame at fixed t, assert exact path output; any parameter nudge fails CI (`npm run test` already runs on every push); (3) sizes below ~32px (`xs`/`sm` rail marks) KEEP the current simple two-circle orb — hexes mush at tiny sizes; 3D form takes over `lg`+; (4) reduced-motion renders a static frame; (5) on ship, promote this item to a locked "Pip Visual Spec Rule" near the top of CLAUDE.md in the same commit.
   - Status: **✅ SHIPPED to `main` June 10 2026 PM** — built by Sonnet Patch from the frozen spec, reviewed line-by-line by the main session (3 review fixes: live `stateRef` so state changes reach the rAF loop, speaking pulse on the spec'd 0.42s clock, `.pip.pip3d > svg { animation:none }` so classic CSS breathe never fights the JS frames). `PipOrb` routes `lg/xl/xxl` → `PipOrb3D`; `xs/sm/md` keep the classic orb. Drift lock live: 35 tests in `pip3dGeometry.test.js` incl. output hashes. `--accent-hi` token added to all four palettes. Verified rendering live in the real app via headless browser before ship. **Same-day approved tweaks (Chris, in his words):** ring spin 0.45→0.18 (nausea), Home hero orb always `xxl` + `.pip.xxl` 132→160px, and state-tint fix — `.pip.thinking`/`.pip.alert` now also override `--accent-hi`/`--accent-deep` (via color-mix) so the 3D form retints as ONE color instead of mixed red/teal. **Round 2 same day:** `motionScale 0.4` (see frozen list) + pulse rings (sonar/heartbeat ::before/::after) suppressed on `.pip3d` — the hex ring IS the ring; classic small orbs keep them. **Round 3 same day (final):** breath 2.4→4.8s + motionScale back to 1.0 — Chris identified the breath, not the rotation, as the nauseating motion; spin stays 0.18.

**45. Hex design language spread — Pip's geometric motif as subtle details across the app** — *(**✅ v1 SHIPPED to `main` June 11 2026** — `src/lib/hexMotif.jsx` (hexPathD + HexSignature + HexPulse + HexField + HexLattice, 9 tests) wired into: account cards + Quick Tasks tray + zero-accounts empty state (AccountsView), Gauge project cards, kanban task cards (StandingBoardView), cadence event cards (cadenceShared), PipCard 5-cell signature, PipView thinking dots → HexPulse, SummarizeStreamingOverlay HexPulse, Home hero HexField. Built by Sonnet Patch in a worktree, reviewed line-by-line, cherry-picked. Pip Visual Spec untouched (drift tests green). **Tier 2 SHIPPED June 11 2026 (same day):** auth-screen `HexField` (AuthView backdrop, peak 0.1); **icon export** — `scripts/render-pip-icon.js` renders `public/icon-512.png` + `icon-192.png` + `docs/assets/pip-logo.svg` from the FROZEN `pip3dGeometry.buildPipFrame(1.1)` (never hand-drawn; rerun the script + `npm run docs:pdf` if Pip ever legitimately changes), PDFs regenerated; **unread glow tie-in** — PipCard's 5-cell signature renders amber (`--c-yellow`) at 0.5 peak while unread, reverts to accent 0.30 on read; **loader ring** — moot, `PipLoader` already renders `PipOrb size="lg"` = the full 3D form with ring. Opacities (0.13/0.30) are the tuning knobs — expect a tune pass once Chris sees it on his phone. Original spec follows; queued June 11 2026, Chris: "his new geometric ring should have subtle details spread out amongst the app"; **mockup live at `public/mockups/hex-spread.html`, served at `folioshq.com/mockups/hex-spread.html`** — 6 surfaces in situ with Work/Life mode toggle, same frozen Bold Hex geometry as the orb; sample names fictionalized since the URL is public/unauthenticated)* Extend the Bold Hex visual language beyond the orb as **presence cues** — hexes appear where Pip is working or speaking, never as generic decoration. Candidates, in priority order:
   - **Tier 1 (signature moments):** `PipLoader` auth/loading screen → small hex torus ring spinner (first screen every morning); Pip **thinking indicators** (chat typing dots + `SummarizeStreamingOverlay`) → 3–4 tiny hexes opening/closing on the breath clock; **`PipCard` header strip** → faint hex-edge accent so every Pip-authored card carries the signature; **empty states** → ultra-faint hex lattice watermark (~2–3% opacity) behind the copy.
   - **Tier 2 (ambient):** Home hero backdrop — barely-there radial hex fade behind the big orb (dark theme especially); auth/sign-in screen hex-ring backdrop; **favicon + PWA icon + `docs/assets/pip-logo.svg`** still show the old two-circle orb — export a static Bold Hex frame so the home-screen icon + PDF headers match the new Pip; amber unread glow on Pip cards → subtle hex-edged pulse instead of round halo.
   - **Explicitly skip:** progress bars, buttons, and the PipGlyph status set — that's where signature tips into wallpaper (the "don't make it busy" lesson).
   - **Guardrails (locked at queue time):** ONE shared primitive — reuse the hex math from `src/lib/pip3dGeometry.js` (or a thin `hexMotif` helper built on it), no per-surface reimplementations (App Coherence Rule); motifs are decoration, NEVER a redrawn Pip — only `PipOrb` renders Pip himself (Visual Spec Rule untouched); colors from accent tokens only (Life-mode orange + both themes inherit free); reduced-motion renders static; breath-clock sync (4.8s) where animated so the whole app breathes together.
   - **HEX GRAMMAR v1 — the structured format (June 11 2026, per Chris: "I want these subtle details throughout the app, all different tabs… accounts cards get a touch of it and project cards and task and cadence cards also get the same thing since all of them currently have the same structure"; mockup section "One grammar, every card" in `public/mockups/hex-spread.html`):** four primitives from one helper (`src/lib/hexMotif.jsx` or similar, built on the frozen hex geometry):
     1. **`hexSignature(n, peak)`** — fading corner chain (each cell ×0.58 the previous), bottom-right of cards, NEVER animated. **Cell count encodes authorship:** **5 cells @ ~0.30 peak = Pip-authored** (PipCard, operator panel, prepped blocks); **3 cells @ ~0.13 peak = user content** (account cards, Gauge project cards, cadence cards, kanban task cards — one identical treatment across the shared card anatomy). Status colors stay on the left edge as today; hexes are ALWAYS accent-colored — two channels, never mixed.
     2. **`hexLattice`** — uniform watermark ~0.045, empty states only, static.
     3. **`hexField`** — radial-falloff lattice (peak ~0.16 fading to 0), Home hero behind the orb + auth screen, static.
     4. **`hexPulse`** — breathing cells on the 4.8s clock; ONLY where Pip actively works: loader (ring) + thinking indicators (3 staggered cells).
     **Placement rules:** cards get the signature, **rows NEVER do** — a panel of dense rows gets ONE chain on the panel (50 rows, one chain); where a Mark glyph already provides identity (view headers, nav), no hex motif (one identity per surface); opacities are dark-theme values — re-tune for light theme at build and verify both (Theme Rule).

   **EXECUTION PROTOCOL (read before building any batch):**
   1. One batch = one Sonnet Patch run in a worktree, phrased per the Patch gotchas ("YOU are Patch — EXECUTE NOW; don't end turn until git commit succeeds"). Main session reviews line-by-line, ticks boxes in the SAME commit, ships on Chris's "push."
   2. DB changes apply to prod via MCP migration + fold into `schema.sql` in the same batch.
   3. After ALL batches: run a final verification sweep — one agent re-checks every ticked box against the code (the "audit-the-fix" pass). Untickable boxes get re-opened, never deleted.
   4. Sanity-Pass Rule applies to every fix (esp. the silent-failure surfaces: RLS, prompts, cron, localStorage).

**48. Pip cost-effectiveness — token spend audit + fixes (queued June 12 2026, after Chris flagged "he flies through tokens now")** — *(PARTIAL — spend cap wired into operator-run June 16 2026; remaining items below.)* Built on the new `folio_pip_usage` logging from item 47 Batch 1. NOTE: `folio_pip_usage` historical data only covers usage since item 47's ship (`fa4bf2b`, June 12) — re-pull after a week for a true per-endpoint breakdown. Cost constants in `api/_pipUsage.js` are CORRECT (haiku: in:0.1/out:0.5, sonnet: in:0.3/out:1.5) — an earlier CLAUDE.md entry called them "1000× wrong" but that was fixed before this session; ignore the stale language.
   - **SHIPPED June 16 2026:** `overDailySpendCap(admin, userId)` wired into `api/operator-run.js` — called after `pickMovedAccounts`; if over cap, `moved = []` (all deep passes skipped, roll-up still runs on prior state). Uses service-role admin client with explicit `user_id` filter, which is equivalent to a user-scoped read for this purpose.
   - **REMAINING (not yet built):** (3) **`pip-state-refresh` gating on actual change** — it has three triggers stacking to 60–130 calls/day (6h periodic top-10 batch, chat-open 20-stale sweep, manual resync button); gate auto-triggers on activity/correction log actually moving since last refresh + add daily localStorage throttle to the chat-open trigger → cuts ~70–90% with zero freshness loss. Evaluate folding/dropping it entirely given operator-run now covers per-account state. (4) **On-demand draft emails** — today operator-run pre-drafts follow-up emails for every flagged account (the email is the biggest output chunk at 5× input price) but most pre-drafts are never sent; defer to when Chris clicks "Draft" in the OperatorPanel. (5) **Conditional output fields** — emit `agenda` only when an upcoming meeting exists, `delta` only when prior state exists; saves output tokens on quiet accounts. (6) **Skip roll-up on a genuinely quiet night** — carry yesterday's report forward + a one-line "nothing new" stamp instead of a fresh Sonnet call.
   - **THE FIX SET (scoped, low-risk):** ~~(1) correct the 4 cost constants~~ DONE prior session. ~~(2) Wire spend cap into operator-run~~ DONE June 16. (3)–(6) above are the remaining levers.
   - **STRATEGY (the Opus answer to "more cost-effective without compromising Pip's intelligence," June 12 2026):** the durable levers, captured so they don't die in chat — **(1) Prompt-cache discipline:** the static block (`PIP_PERSONA`+formatting+fewshots) must stay byte-stable; every persona edit (e.g. the item-46 anti-sycophancy line) busts the cache and re-bills full input. Audit which surfaces actually hit cache (chat does ~3.4k cache-read; `pip-state-refresh` + `pip` Haiku show **0 cache** — they pay full input every call). **(2) Right-size context per surface, don't dump everything:** intelligence comes from the RIGHT context, not MORE — trim per-account context to what the surface needs (the parity rule says wire a field to both paths, NOT that every field goes to every surface). **(3) Tier by reasoning need, not by habit:** Sonnet only where semantic judgment matters (summarize project-matching, chat, daily brief synthesis); Haiku for extraction/compression/classification (already mostly done in Batch 1). **(4) Event-driven over timer-driven:** recompute state on real signals (new meeting, task close, correction logged), never on a clock — kills the `pip-state-refresh` waste class and is the operator-run signal-gating principle generalized. **(5) Cache/dedupe expensive once-a-day outputs** (brief, operator report) — already saved to DB; never regenerate for the same inputs. **(6) Make spend VISIBLE + capped** (the fixed tile + a real per-day cap that gates the biggest spender) so cost can't silently run away again. Full reasoning in the June 12 chat; this is the durable checklist.
   - **SONNET→HAIKU AUDIT (June 12 2026 — answer to "anywhere I use Sonnet I could use Haiku?"):** 7 Sonnet surfaces exist (`operator-run`, summarize, chat, daily brief, `profile-synthesis`, QBR, `generate-questions`). Verdict: **KEEP Sonnet** on operator-run / summarize / chat / daily brief (real judgment — you'd feel the downgrade) and on profile-synthesis + QBR (too rare to save anything, high-stakes output). **Only `generate-questions` is a clean Haiku candidate** (background drip, lowest stakes, already auto-degrades to Haiku over the spend cap). The obvious extraction/transform jobs are ALREADY Haiku (Batch 1 reroutes + per-account brief/email/terminology/state-refresh/leadership-readout). KEY: every Sonnet surface reads a per-surface env override (`PIP_QUESTIONS_MODEL`/`PIP_QBR_MODEL`/`PIP_CHAT_MODEL`/`PIP_OPERATOR_MODEL`/`PIP_DAILY_BRIEF_MODEL`/`PIP_PROFILE_MODEL`), so tier is **A/B-testable in Vercel env with NO deploy** — flip `PIP_QUESTIONS_MODEL=claude-haiku-4-5-20251001`, live with it a week, keep it if quality holds. Tiering is NOT where the real money is (the easy moves are done) — volume/caching/gating are.
   - **OPERATOR-RUN COST-REDUCTION PASS (June 12 2026 — Chris kept it on Sonnet, wants usage down without dumbing it down). MEASURE FIRST against the first night of logs, then cut.** Cost = (deep passes × per-pass tokens) + 1 roll-up. Levers, ranked, all Sonnet-quality-preserving: **Tier 1 (≈zero quality cost):** (1) **Draft follow-up emails on-demand, not draft-ahead** — the email is the biggest *output* chunk (output = 5× input price) and most pre-drafts are never sent; defer to when Chris clicks "draft" (same Sonnet, fresher context). DECIDING QUESTION: does he actually send the pre-drafts? If rarely → free win. (2) **Conditional output fields** — emit `agenda` only when a meeting's upcoming, `delta` only when prior state exists (email already conditional). (3) **Skip the roll-up on a genuinely quiet night** — carry yesterday's report forward + one-line "nothing new" instead of a fresh Sonnet call. (4) **Right-size per-account context** — the uncacheable bulk; trim renderAccountContext to decision-relevant fields (last 1-2 meetings + tone, overdue/commitment tasks, champions/blockers, in-flight projects) — careful not to cut signal. **Tier 2 (small tradeoff, bigger savings):** (5) **Delta-update instead of full re-read** — feed prior state + "what changed since" and ask to UPDATE, not rebuild; far less in/out for barely-moved accounts (also a continuity *gain*). (6) **Deep sweep 2-3×/week + heuristic-light (no-LLM) the other nights.** **Rejected:** batching many accounts per call (attention dilution + output-limit); longer cache TTL (can't span 24h). Caching the shared user-context (operating_context/profile/glossary, ~3k tok) into the cached system block across the 8 passes — separate already-agreed win (currently re-billed 8× in the user message at gatherAndRun ~line 519). Build Tier 1 first; delta-updates as follow-up.

**36. Pip follow-up questions (conversational Teach Pip)** — *(✅ SHIPPED June 16 2026)* When the user answers one of Pip's questions (drip / "Teach Pip" / Catch Up), Pip fires a follow-up that digs into that specific answer ~60% of the time, making Teach Pip feel like a real conversation rather than a form.
   - **Built:** new `api/followup-question.js` Haiku endpoint (JWT auth, `logPipUsage` wired, Anthropic client inside try-catch, `maxDuration:30`). Gates: answer must be ≥30 chars, no chaining (follow-up on a follow-up blocked by `source === "followup"` check), terminology questions never get follow-ups. Inserts: `source:'followup'`, `priority:10`, `category:'biographical'`, `trigger_context: "follow-up to question " + questionId`. `PIP_FOLLOWUP_MODEL` env override available.
   - **`usePipDripQuestions.js`:** inner `fetch` callback renamed → `loadRows` throughout (critical: frees the global `fetch` name for use inside `triggerFollowup`). Queue and throttle queries updated to `.in("source", ["gap_observed", "followup"])` so follow-ups surface in the drip queue. `triggerFollowup(question, answerText)` is fire-and-forget (gets session token, calls `/api/followup-question`, calls `loadRows()` on success to surface immediately). `answerAndCount` calls it with `Math.random() < 0.6` gate after every answered question.
   - **Cost guard:** ≤1 Haiku call per answer; follow-up rows count toward daily cap (part of `["gap_observed","followup"]` window) but NOT toward the `QUEUE_SOFT_CAP` in `generate-questions` (which still only counts `gap_observed` — follow-ups don't block gap detection).

**37. Pip should reason about the user's org structure (departments/teams)** — *(✅ SHIPPED June 16 2026 — quick-win half)* `api/generate-questions.js` now splits accounts into two labeled sections before sending to Sonnet: "YOUR OWN INTERNAL TEAMS / DEPARTMENTS (you ARE part of these — they are NOT external relationships to manage)" and "YOUR MANAGED ACCOUNTS (external suppliers, partners, clients — you maintain the relationship)". Added ORG STRUCTURE system-prompt rule instructing Pip to never ask about relationships a department's existence already answers. User message updated to show counts ("N managed, N internal teams"). Prevents the "who owns the MSO relationship?" class of questions when an MSO Team dept is visible.
   - **Deferred (bigger half):** explicit LINK between a department and the accounts/segment it covers; parity across detect-terminology + chat + summarize. Those surfaces still get a flat account list. Wire when the explicit dept↔account link data model lands.

**38. Pip must distinguish accounts I MANAGE from accounts I'm only PROJECT-involved in (MSO ownership)** — *(✅ SHIPPED June 16 2026 — primary surfaces)* Pip no longer treats "not mine" accounts (where `owner_user_id !== userId`) as Chris's relationship to manage. Uses the existing "Mine / Not mine" toggle on the account header to read `owner_user_id`.
   - **`api/operator-run.js`:** accounts select now includes `owner_user_id`. `renderAccountContext` emits `RELATIONSHIP_OWNER: NO — this account is managed by someone else; this user is project-involved only` when ownership doesn't match. `ACCOUNT_SYSTEM` prompt rule: *if RELATIONSHIP_OWNER: NO, do NOT suggest outreach, follow-up emails, cadence nudges, or "you should reach out" items — only surface project-level work (tasks, Gauge projects, deliverables)*. `userId` threaded as 9th param into `renderAccountContext` calls.
   - **`src/views/home/HomeView.jsx`:** `coldAccounts` computation skips accounts where `owner_user_id && userId && owner_user_id !== userId`. `anomalySignals` forEach does the same. MSO accounts set to "Not mine" now vanish from cold-contact nudges and off-cadence anomaly signals on Home.
   - **Remaining surfaces (not yet done):** portfolio-brief, leadership-readout, and the draft-ahead section still treat all accounts equally — those are lower-frequency surfaces and can be addressed in a follow-up pass when the dept↔account link data model lands (item 37 bigger half).

**39. Pip speed — stream the meeting summary as it writes** — *(✅ SHIPPED June 10 2026 PM inside Game Plan Phase 1.1d — two-phase output: prose recap streams live into SummarizeStreamingOverlay, ===PLAN=== delimiter, JSON plan parses on completion; server already streamed any mode so api/pip.js untouched.)* The slowest user-facing Pip surface is meeting **summarize** (`mode:"summary"`, Sonnet, `max_tokens:3072`, **buffered** — you hit "End & Summarize" and stare at a spinner until the whole structured plan is generated). Chris's pick: make Pip's written recap **stream onto the screen word-by-word** (like Ask Pip chat already does via `streamPip`) so he's reading within ~1s instead of waiting. Keep Sonnet quality (don't downgrade to Haiku; don't hard-cap length).
   - **The wrinkle:** the summarize call returns a structured JSON object (the plan that drives `PipSummarizePreview`), not prose — you can't usefully stream raw JSON tokens to the UI. So this is a real change to the summarize flow, not a flag flip. Likely shape: a **two-phase** flow — stream a readable prose recap first (visible immediately), then resolve the structured plan and open the preview modal — OR restructure the model output so the prose recap comes first as plain text and the JSON plan follows a delimiter, streaming the prose portion live and parsing the plan on completion. Decide at build; watch cost (don't double the Sonnet call needlessly — Chris is cost-sensitive).
   - Touches `summarizeDraftPip` (`src/lib/pip.js`), the `summary` mode in `api/pip.js`, and the callers (CadenceHub / CadenceMeetingMode / AccountDetail) + `PipSummarizePreview`. Other slow surfaces (daily brief) stay as-is — they're cached once/day.

**40. **41. In-meeting per-project note blocks — split-screen meeting mode** — *(✅ SHIPPED June 10 2026 PM — rebuilt fresh on `main` by this session; Chris's own earlier build was stranded unpushed in another session and never reached `main`. Built per the locked design: desktop split (projects pane ~42% left, per-project note field on each discussed card, general notes right), mobile Notes|Projects full-width toggle, Items+People collapsible under projects, inline add-contact preserved in both layouts (Chris's explicit mid-meeting requirement; shared `AddContactInline`), un-discuss confirms before discarding typed notes. Pip: per-project notes injected into summarize as labeled provenance blocks with a route-to-this-project instruction; noted projects auto-count as discussed and toward the trivial-draft skip threshold; all three summarize callers verified. Docs + PDFs updated. **Deferred follow-ups → Game Plan Phase 1.1:** group plan-modal rows by project in `PipSummarizePreview`; auto-suggest a Gauge status pulse from a project's notes.)* In `CadenceMeetingMode`, clicking a project in the sidebar today just flags it `discussed` (teal → `discussedProjectIds` → Pip routing hint at summarize). Chris wants per-project notes captured *within the meeting*, separate from the main freeform notes, so Pip knows which notes belong to which project.
   - **Layout (split screen):** the meeting body splits in two — one side the **projects panel** (project cards), the other side the **general notes** (current textarea, unchanged). The per-project note field lives **inside each project card itself** — nothing animates/moves over. Click a card → activates "discussed" + reveals its own note field (+ optionally its task list via item 30's inline actions). Today's sidebar already gives the two-pane bones; this rebalances toward ~50/50 and makes projects primary.
   - **DECISIONS LOCKED (June 2026):**
     - **Mobile:** a top **"Notes | Projects" toggle** — two full-width modes (type general notes in one, flip to Projects and tap a card to type its notes). Same two-spaces model, stacked in time on a phone.
     - **Left/projects panel:** **Projects is the default content**, with **Open Items + People as small collapsible sections beneath** — stays project-focused but you can still tick an item / check attendees.
     - **"Discussed" is implicit:** engaging a card (opening its note field) marks it discussed = the routing signal Pip needs; the note text itself is **optional** (you can discuss a project and type nothing). Never forced.
     - **Moving a chunk of general notes into a project: NOT built** — Chris will copy/paste manually. No select-text→send-to-project affordance.
     - **Un-discuss:** confirm before discarding a project's typed notes — a stray tap must never nuke notes.

   - **Data model:** new `folio_meetings.project_notes jsonb` = `{ [projectId]: noteText }`. Keep `notes` as the general blob. Structured > parsing one delimited blob — clean provenance for Pip.
   - **The payoff:** summarize gets project-scoped notes keyed by project → Pip routes that project's action items to *that* project precisely, and can **auto-suggest a Gauge "Latest update" status pulse** from its notes (ties into shipped `gauge_projects.status_updates`). Plan modal could group rows by project. Parity rule: wire `project_notes` into both `pip.js` summarize payload + the preview flow.

**42. Work ↔ Life mode — Folios becomes a personal Pip-first assistant (Life module)** — *(**PHASE 1 SHIPPED to `main` + live, June 10 2026.** Phase 2 = honey-do brain, next.)* The strategic turn: Folios isn't a SaaS to sell, it's Chris's own assistant. Pip is the product; "Folios" (work) is one lens, and a new **Life** lens sits beside it. One app, one Pip brain, two modes; unified only in the daily brief. Picture: **Work/Life (top toggle) → modules (Accounts, Gauge … + new Life module) → workspaces (account slices, work-side only).**
   - **PHASE 1 SHIPPED (June 10 2026):** mode system (`useMode` + `index.html` `data-mode` pre-mount script + `[data-mode="life"]` token overrides), `ModeToggle` (desktop bottom-left by user menu; mobile header; +Account moved to top of Accounts view both platforms; rail Add pill removed), mode-scoped nav (Life shows only Home), `life_items` table (RLS, prod + `schema.sql` + `supabase/life_items.sql`), `useLifeItems`, `src/lib/lifeLadder.js` (VIP heads-up ladder + annual recurrence + honey-do aging/complexity sort), `LifeHome` (Upcoming / Honey-do / Soccer moved from work Home), `AddLifeItemModal` (auto-flags VIP events). **Final palette: dusty-blue surfaces + faded DUSTY-ORANGE accent** (Pip orb + all highlights; the orb just reads `--accent`). Work mode byte-for-byte unchanged. **Fast-follows (not yet done):** NL "tell Pip" capture (structured quick-add only today), Life→daily-brief fusion (unified day), VIP-ladder → real reminder banners/push, Life bottom nav is single-Home for now.
   - **PHASE 2 (NEXT, the headline feature) — the honey-do BRAIN:** Pip as a home-project partner — how-to coaching, materials/tools to buy, step-by-step, troubleshooting mid-project, complexity reasoning. Deep-dive with Chris before building. (Honey-do today only remembers + prioritizes.)
   - **Mode system:** a `data-mode="work"|"life"` attribute on `<html>` (parallel to `data-theme`), persisted to `localStorage` (`folio_mode`), via a `useMode()` hook modeled on `useTheme()`. Default work. Pre-mount inline script in `index.html` sets it (no flash), same as theme.
   - **Theme (dusty blue):** Life mode reskins via `[data-mode="life"]` CSS-var overrides in `index.html` — accent + shades swap from work green to **dusty blue (light→dark shades, mirroring how work is shades of green)**. Reuses the token architecture (every `C.*` is a `var(--…)`), so the whole app recolors instantly with no remount. Must work in BOTH dark and light themes (so `[data-theme][data-mode]` combinations). Green stays canonical for work; blue = off the clock — a psychological signal.
   - **Toggle placement (LOCKED):** **desktop** — bottom-left by the CV/avatar in the user-menu corner of the rail. **Mobile** — the toggle takes the global header spot where **+Account** currently lives; **+Account moves up into the top of the Accounts tab** (it's account-specific anyway).
   - **Life module + Life Home (the 3 cards):** (1) **Upcoming** — what's on the calendar soon (appointments + events). (2) **Honey-do list** — ordered by a blend of how long it's been open (aging) + job complexity. (3) **Soccer** — `SportsCard` MOVED out of the work Home into Life Home (de-clutters work too).
   - **Data model:** new `life_items` table, RLS scoped to `auth.uid()`. One table, `kind` in (`appointment`|`event`|`todo`): common cols `title, notes, date, time, location, status, opened_at, complexity, recurrence` (e.g. annual for events), `importance` tier, `lead_ladder` (or derive from importance). Fold into `schema.sql` + new `supabase/life_items.sql`; apply to prod via MCP.
   - **Important events — VIP heads-up ladder (LOCKED: tiers-with-defaults + Pip auto-flags the obvious ones):** events carry an **importance tier**; VIP (anniversary, spouse/kids birthdays, Christmas) get a **multi-stage escalating ladder** — ~3wk soft ("start thinking") → 1wk ("got a plan?") → 3d ("order now so it ships in time") → 1d + day-of (hard). Normal events get a short few-day runway. VIP nudges are more insistent (cost of forgetting is high). **Recurs annually** — set the date once, Pip carries it forward forever. Pip infers importance from title ("anniversary"/"wife's birthday" obviously high-stakes); user can override. (Phase 2: Pip helps with the gift — ideas + order-by dates.)
   - **Capture:** plain-language to Pip ("dentist Tuesday at 3", "honey-do: rebuild the back gate") → filed into the right `kind`. Phase 1 may start with a structured quick-add and layer NL parse as a fast-follow.
   - **Phase 1 = the STRUCTURE (skeleton + blue coat):** mode toggle + dusty-blue theme + Life module nav + Life Home (3 cards, sports moved) + `life_items` schema/hook + quick-add + the VIP ladder surfaced on Life Home. Work mode stays 100% unchanged (Life is additive). **Phase 2 = the honey-do BRAIN** (the part Chris most wants): Pip as a home-project partner — complexity reasoning, how-to coaching, materials/steps, troubleshooting mid-project. Deep-dive after the structure ships.
   - **Pip parity:** eventually Life items feed the daily brief so the morning read is the WHOLE day (work + life). Phase 1 keeps Life self-contained; brief fusion is the first fast-follow.

<details><summary>original spec</summary>

**Gauge project "Latest update" pulse log** — a quick status-update field on each Gauge project, distinct from the existing `notes` blob (notes = durable scratchpad; updates = timestamped running heartbeat). **Design locked:**
    - **Storage:** `status_updates jsonb default '[]'` on `gauge_projects` — array of `{ body, at (ISO), by (user email) }`, newest-first. No new table, no join; rides the existing `updateProject` path. The array *is* the history.
    - **Model: append-only.** Each save prepends a new timestamped entry; the previous becomes history. `at` auto-stamped on save; `by` auto-captured (matters for Leader view). Typo fixes happen in the project edit box, not inline.
    - **Expanded card (GaugeView):** one-line "Latest update" field showing the current pulse + muted relative timestamp ("Updated 2h ago · Jun 4"). Type + Enter/Save prepends.
    - **Edit box (ProjectModal):** "Status history" read-only list — every past update with timestamp + author.
    - **Pip wiring (parity rule — both paths):** inject latest + the prior two (for momentum sense) into `pipContext.js` (chat) AND `pip.js` (summarize), plus daily/portfolio brief, leadership readout, and cadence pre-call brief. Lets briefs say "All Star — latest: 'waiting on legal sign-off' (Jun 3)." Keep it cheap: latest + last 2 only.
    - SQL: new `supabase/gauge_project_status_updates.sql` + fold into canonical `schema.sql`. Docs: update `docs/product-overview.md` (Gauge capability) + `docs/upgrades.md` entry on ship.

</details>
