34. **Pip Autonomous Operator — ~~nightly loop~~ MANUAL-TRIGGER loop + materialized operator state + dynamic Pip cards everywhere** — *(Phases 1, 2 & 2.5 SHIPPED June 8 2026. **⚠️ TRIGGER CHANGED June 17 2026: the nightly Vercel cron was RETIRED — the operator now runs ONLY when Chris taps "Run Pip's pass" on Home.** Cost decision: it ran every morning whether or not he opened the app, and the report rarely changed his day. `vercel.json` `crons` entry removed; `api/operator-run.js` now also accepts a user JWT (scopes the run to that user) so the browser button can trigger it without the cron secret; `OperatorRunButton` on Home drives it. The engine/output/state below are otherwise unchanged — wherever this spec says "cron" / "nightly" / "overnight," read "on manual trigger." See the June 17 2026 handoff.)* turn Pip from a pull-triggered advisor into a scheduled agent that works the book of business and pre-fills every Pip surface in the app. The morning brief is the read-only *head* of this; the loop is the body. **Design locked:**

    - **Phase 1 status (built):** the engine + the Home operator report. Built: `api/operator-run.js` (cron endpoint — CRON_SECRET-gated, service-role, runs every morning, signal-gated deep passes capped at 8/run on Sonnet **run in parallel waves of 4** (`maxDuration:60`; sequential calls blew past Vercel's function timeout and killed the run after ~5 accounts before it wrote the report — fixed June 8 2026), one portfolio roll-up call, propose-only); **(weekend opt-in gate was built then PULLED June 8 2026 at Chris's request — caused testing confusion and saved only pennies; the loop now runs daily, signal-gating alone controls cost);** `vercel.json` cron at `0 9 * * *` (~5am ET); schema (`supabase/pip_operator.sql` — operator_* columns on `folio_pip_account_state` + new `folio_operator_reports` table, **applied to prod via MCP + folded into schema.sql**); `src/hooks/useOperatorReport.js`; registered in `scripts/test-api-imports.js`; docs + PDFs. **Deploy state (LIVE):** `CRON_SECRET` is set in Vercel and the cron fires daily (~5am ET); `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` + `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` already set; `OPERATOR_TZ` (default America/New_York) + `PIP_OPERATOR_MODEL` (default claude-sonnet-4-6) left at defaults. Manual run: `GET /api/operator-run?secret=<CRON_SECRET>&user=<uuid>` — **a human's `?secret=` query call always runs** (the gone weekend-gate + no skip), the cron uses Bearer auth. **The report is rebuilt each run from the whole prepped book** (this run's fresh deep passes + accounts still carrying recent operator state, last 4 days) so a quiet day still yields a Home report for ~1 roll-up call; it **never clobbers a good same-day report with an empty one** (clobber bug fixed June 8 — report keyed `(user, local date)`, only written when there's content). **Operator REPORT output is structured** `{ headline, opening, sections:[{kind:fire|watch|win|signal, items:[{account_name, line, action, has_draft}]}] }`, stored headline→`headline`, opening→`report_prose`, sections→`plan_items` (jsonb). Per-account deep pass (`ACCOUNT_SYSTEM`) returns `{ headline, situation, risks[], draft_email, proposed_moves[], agenda, delta }` → operator_* columns.

    - **Phase 2.5 (built — unified Pip card + Home redo, June 8 2026):** shared `src/components/PipCard.jsx` shell — one anatomy everywhere: HEAD (✦ Pip label + timestamp, a high-level **headline**, a density row of count chips) always visible; BODY collapsed by default ("Show details ▾"). `OperatorPanel` composes it (head = `operator_headline` + `N risks · draft · N moves`; body = situation/delta/risks/draft/moves). **Amber unread-notification glow** (`pip-unread` + `pipUnreadPulse` keyframe, `--c-yellow-glow` token both themes): card pulses amber + "NEW" dot when `operator_generated_at` is newer than this device's last-open (localStorage `folio_op_read_<acct>`), clears on expand. New per-account `operator_headline` column (prompt + migration applied to prod + schema.sql + pip_operator.sql). **Home redo → dashboard of cards** (iterated live with Chris over several rounds; final shape): the operator REPORT output is structured (see Phase 1 status). HomeView renders, top-to-bottom: greeting + **centered heartbeat orb** (`.pip.heartbeat`, ~3.4s slowed thump-thump-rest, reduced-motion-gated; `PipOrb heartbeat` prop) → a **"✦ Pip" read card** (the Pip-voiced `opening` paragraph + worked/time) → a **full-width, bigger "Today" card** (the `fire` section) → **This week / Pattern / Good news** as separate cards in a **2-up grid** (stacked mobile), content-only (a section with no items doesn't render). Every section row is tappable (account Glow + Open + inline **"✦ Draft ready"** that copies the drafted email — drafts/commitments fused into rows, no separate cards). The short Pip one-liner under the orb (`pickHeroLine`, rewritten to short/accurate/varied lines from real counts — *"Busy one today. Let's dig in."* / *"Slow day — good time to warm up a cold account."*) is **dropped whenever an operator report is active** (`operatorActive` flag), since the read card says it better; it only shows on the fallback/no-operator path. Commitment-nudge + live-daily-brief cards suppressed when a report has content. **Pip personality** dialed up in `REPORT_SYSTEM` (dry wit + slightly anxious + loyal, examples + a never-say-filler rule) concentrated in the `headline` + `opening`; section `line`s stay tight. Per-account fallback (no operator state yet) = lightweight heuristic head-only `PipCard` on the account Overview. **Not yet propagated:** the unified PipCard + glow onto Cadence/Gauge (those still use the Phase-2 read-only blocks); Calendar strip; PWA push.

    - **Phase 2 status (built — dynamic cards):** the materialized state is read by every relevant surface (no extra LLM call on open; data already loads via `usePipAccountState`'s `select("*")`). Built: shared `src/components/OperatorPanel.jsx` (per-account lens — situation, "since last run" delta, risk chips, drafted email Copy/Mail, proposed moves each with **+ Add task / Dismiss**; approve creates a `folio_task` and marks the move `status:applied` in the jsonb so it doesn't reappear; dismiss marks `status:dismissed`) wired into **AccountDetail** (between header and tabs); **CadenceHub** read-only "Pip prepped this overnight" block (situation + suggested agenda) above the cadence brief on account cadences; **GaugeView/PipGaugeCard** "✦ Pip proposes" cross-account decision queue (flattens pending `operator_proposed_moves` across `pipAcctState.states`, approve → `insertTask` + mark applied). All guarded to render nothing until `operator_generated_at` exists, so the app is visually unchanged until the loop first runs. **Remaining slivers (NOT built):** Calendar plan-projection strip (deliberately deferred — would duplicate Home's report + risks the "don't make it busy" lesson; needs `userId` threaded into the presentational `CalendarView`); optional PWA push companion ("Pip has your operator report ✦", content stays in-app).

    - **The loop:** Vercel cron runs nightly, weekday mornings (Sun→Thu nights). Sweeps the portfolio via the *existing* Pip endpoints — no new permissions, no email/corporate integration (deliberately off the table: compliance + Chris can get in trouble forwarding customer data). For each account that *moved*, runs a deep per-account pass (read account → decide next action → draft the artifact → propose assignee/agenda). Accounts that didn't move ride the cheap compressed path. The loop is **not latency-bound**, so it can afford per-account reasoning the synchronous brief can't (the brief is one compressed Sonnet call because you're staring at a spinner; the loop is unhurried batch depth).

    - **The loop:** Vercel cron runs nightly, weekday mornings (Sun→Thu nights). Sweeps the portfolio via the *existing* Pip endpoints — no new permissions, no email/corporate integration (deliberately off the table: compliance + Chris can get in trouble forwarding customer data). For each account that *moved*, runs a deep per-account pass (read account → decide next action → draft the artifact → propose assignee/agenda). Accounts that didn't move ride the cheap compressed path. The loop is **not latency-bound**, so it can afford per-account reasoning the synchronous brief can't (the brief is one compressed Sonnet call because you're staring at a spinner; the loop is unhurried batch depth).

    - **Materialized operator state (the core architecture):** the loop writes a per-account "operator state" object to Supabase — extends existing `pip_account_state` / `folio_account_snapshots` (decide `pip_account_state` extension vs. new `folio_operator_state` at build). Holds: situation, flagged risks, **pre-drafted follow-up email(s)**, proposed task/project moves, pre-built cadence agenda, and a **"what changed since last run" delta**. This object is the single source of truth.

    - **Dynamic Pip cards = lenses on one brain:** every Pip surface *reads the materialized state* instead of making its own LLM call on open. Same brain, different window per surface:
        - **Home** → the "operator report": prioritized plan with pre-drafted artifacts to approve/adjust/send (evolves the daily brief from "what's happening" → "what's happening + I drafted it").
        - **Cadence Hub** → pre-built agenda + queued drafts for that account, instant (replaces the current on-open Haiku brief call).
        - **Gauge / PipGaugeCard** → proposed project moves as a *decision queue* ("stalled 14d, re-route the legal task to Dana — approve?").
        - **Account detail / Brief Me** → brief pre-written + delta since last look.
        - **Calendar** → the plan projected onto the timeline.
        - Side benefit: this **kills the parity-rule drift** — one materialized brain means no more hand-wiring each new field into both `pipContext.js` *and* `pip.js`. (Until fully migrated, keep both paths fed.)

    - **Three locked guardrails:**
        1. **Signal-gated** — deep passes only on accounts that changed (snapshot/activity diff); the rest stay cheap. If *nothing* moved, there's **no run** — work scales to what changed.
        2. ~~**Weekend opt-in**~~ — *(designed, built, then PULLED June 8 2026 at Chris's request.)* The loop runs every morning regardless of day; signal-gating (guardrail 1) is the sole cost control. Rationale for the pull: the weekend skip created real testing confusion (a Sunday manual run kept "skipping") for only pennies of weekend savings. If ever wanted back, the logic lived in `processUser` (weekday check + `folio_activity`/`folio_tasks` write-since-last-run count).
        3. **Pre-compute once, render everywhere, refresh only on real signal** — cards read pre-computed DB state (a net *cost reduction* on per-surface opens: DB read vs. LLM call). Refresh a card only on a genuine event (new meeting summarized, task closed) — **never on a timer, never on every render.** Respects the render-thrash concern + the "don't make it busy" lesson from the revenue rip. Dynamic ≠ constantly recomputing.

    - **Cost model:** one batched Sonnet sweep/morning over *changed accounts only* (≤12 deep passes + 1 roll-up); per-card opens become DB reads. Net per-surface cost goes *down*.

    - **Push layer (optional companion):** PWA push — "Pip has your operator report ✦" — content stays in-app (no account names in the notification text, nothing on a lockscreen). Turns Pip pull→push without leaking anything.

    - **Positioning:** the leap from "external brain you feed" → "digital chief of staff that works the book." Defensible angle: **institutional relationship memory that runs itself** — the context never walks out the door when an AM leaves.

    - **On ship:** SQL + fold into `schema.sql`; `docs/product-overview.md` (Pip capability) + `docs/upgrades.md` entry + regenerate PDFs. Parity rule applies until the materialized state fully replaces dual-wiring.

A single merged panel would only re-present data already visible. Reopen only if a consolidated view is explicitly wanted.)*

- ✅ **Pip question-pipeline RLS fix (June 2026)** — "Pip, ask me more" (and the terminology drip) silently produced nothing for weeks. Root cause: `api/generate-questions.js` + `api/detect-terminology.js` built a plain **anon** Supabase client and only used the JWT to *validate* the user — they never attached it to the client. Under RLS the anon client read **zero** of the user's accounts (so `generate-questions` bailed with `no_accounts`) and the `folio_pip_questions` insert was **rejected** — confirmed against the live DB (anon insert → *"new row violates row-level security policy"*). Fixed by building the client with `global.headers.Authorization = "Bearer " + token` so every read/insert runs as the user. The whole question pipeline (Lane C terminology + Lane D portfolio) was affected. **See the new "Supabase Server-Client Auth Rule" near the top** to prevent recurrence. Found while debugging Chris's live "questions button hasn't been working" report; the stress-bot's `teachpip` scenario now guards it.
- ✅ **"Off the clock" personal soccer card — Home (June 2026)** — a personal-interest card at the bottom of Home: soccer news (free Guardian RSS, no key) for Man United / Brazil / USMNT / World Cup, plus **live + upcoming scores** via API-Football. `api/sports.js` (server-side so it dodges corporate proxies + keeps the key off the client) fetches RSS + scores, caches in-memory (30 min normally, 120s when a followed team is live), resolves API-Football team ids by name-search (cached), and **degrades to news-only** if the key/API is missing or errors — never breaks Home. `useSportsFeed` hook (5-min client cache) + `src/views/home/SportsCard.jsx` (LIVE ●/min, upcoming kickoff, news headlines with topic chips). Hide toggle: Settings → "Off the clock" (localStorage `folio_show_sports`) + a "hide" link on the card itself. **Needs Vercel env `API_FOOTBALL_KEY`** (free tier, 100 req/day) for scores — news works without it. Registered in `scripts/test-api-imports.js`. *(Scores built defensively without live testing — team-id/free-tier coverage may need a tweak pass once the key's in.)*
- ✅ **Account-merge data-loss fix (June 2026)** — `folio_merge_accounts` predated the `folio_items`→`folio_tasks` unification and the account-updates calendar, so merging an account stranded its action items (`folio_tasks`) and update-log rows (`folio_account_updates`) on the now-inactive source — silent data loss a daily user would only notice when the data went missing. Added re-parenting for both tables; applied to production via migration `fix_merge_accounts_reparent_tasks_and_updates` (which also synced prod to the canonical integer-returning version), and updated `supabase/schema.sql` + `supabase/inactive_and_merge.sql` to match. **Found by inspecting the live DB while building the stress-bot's merge-integrity test** (which now guards it). Also shipped same session: the `account.name.split` ErrorBoundary crash on Accounts/Partners views, guarded in `AccountDetailHeader.jsx` (`account.name || ""`); and `vite.config.js` `sourcemap:"hidden"` so prod crash stacks decode to real `src/` lines. See the Stress-Bot section for the testing harness those came out of.
- ✅ **Teach Pip — on-demand "build his knowledge base" mode (June 2026)** — Chris wanted to deliberately sit down and have Pip fire questions to build context, not just wait for the gentle weekly drip. The `PipCatchUp` "Catch up with Pip" surface already answered the whole queue in a sitting, but (a) it was only reachable when a drip question was already showing, and (b) the generator self-throttles (6h + skip when ≥5 queued), so it ran dry after ~5. Fixes: (1) **`/api/generate-questions` manual mode** — `body { manual:true }` bypasses the backlog cap (`QUEUE_SOFT_CAP`) and asks for a bigger batch (`maxNew` 5→8). (2) **App `teachPipMore()`** — calls the manual endpoint bypassing the 6h localStorage throttle, then `dripHook.refetch()` to pull the new questions in. (3) **PipCatchUp "Pip, ask me more →"** — a persistent footer button (and an empty-state CTA) that runs `teachPipMore` so the session keeps going as long as you like; `onAskMore` prop. (4) **Persistent entry points** — a "Teach Pip about your world" card on Home when no question is queued, and a "Catch up with Pip →" button in Settings → Pip's Questions (both open the global `catchUpOpen`). Everything still flows into `profile_prose` + `folio_pip_facts`, so it compounds into better briefs. No schema changes. **Two follow-up fixes (same day):** (a) the Home "Teach Pip" card's `PipOrb` used `size={18}` (a number) — but `PipOrb`'s `size` is a string enum (`"xs"`…`"xxl"`), so it fell back to the giant centerpiece orb and crushed the card text into a one-word-per-line column on mobile; fixed to `size="sm" isStatic`. (b) **"Pip, ask me more" returned nothing** when the queue was empty: the endpoint runs fine (reads work — it generated 6 on Jun 5), but **Sonnet returns an empty array** once a thorough set is answered ("return empty if nothing insightful" + full already-asked list). Fixed two ways: a manual-mode prompt override telling Pip the user explicitly wants more (don't abstain, dig per-account), AND a **deterministic account-anchored fallback** — if a manual run still yields 0 from the model, generate concrete grounded questions ("Where do things stand with <Account> — what are you trying to move, who decides, what could derail it?", accounts with no objective first, skipping internal teams + already-asked) so manual "ask me more" can never dead-end. Endpoint now returns `{ inserted, modelReturned }` for observability.

- ✅ **Pip plan modal — blank update rows fixed + detach new_task to standalone (June 2026)** — (1) **Bug:** Pip sometimes emitted `update_task` rows on a "discussed" project with no real task to point at → rendered as a useless "CURRENT (empty) → Replace with (blank)" applyable row. `PipSummarizePreview` now sanitizes the incoming plan (shadowing the `plan` prop with a memo): drops `update_task`/`update_item` rows whose target task/item can't be resolved or whose `fields` is empty. Prompt also tightened (`pip.js`): only emit update_* with a real id + concrete change; a discussed project is not itself a task. (2) **Feature:** a `new_task` Pip routed to a project can now be pulled out as a standalone task — the project picker is initialized from `row.project_id` and is the source of truth on apply; selecting "↳ Not in Gauge" clears `project_id` so `applyPipPlan` files it as a standalone task (the fallback path already existed). Row leader reads "New task (standalone)" when detached. No schema changes.
- ✅ **Pip answers visibility + faster re-synthesis (June 2026)** — Chris answered ~6 drip questions in a sitting and saw nothing change → felt like wasted effort. Two fixes: (1) **Re-synthesis throttle 24h → 5 min** in App.jsx so a session of answers folds into `profile_prose` within minutes, not the next day; a "Pip updated what he knows about you ✦" toast confirms it ran. (`answeredSinceSynthesis` resets on `prose_generated_at` change, so no loop; ~$0.004/run.) (2) **Settings "Pip's Questions" section now surfaces** the synthesized `profile_prose` ("What Pip understands about you", read-only via MarkdownText) **and** the raw answered Q&A ("What you've told Pip · N", last 25 from `folio_pip_questions`). Root cause of the complaint: answers were saving fine to `folio_pip_questions.answer_text` and feeding `profile_prose` (injected into every prompt), but had **no UI** — the only visible "What Pip knows" panel showed `folio_pip_facts` glossary facts, not the profile. Partial delivery of item 10 Phase 3 ("What Pip knows about you" in Settings). No schema changes.
- ✅ **Pip structured formatting + status glyphs + daily-brief raw-JSON fix (June 2026)** — (1) **Bug:** the model swap made Sonnet's daily brief overflow `max_tokens:600` → JSON truncated → parse failed → `portfolio-brief.js` fallback dumped the raw JSON string into the UI. Raised budgets on every now-Sonnet JSON endpoint (portfolio-brief 600→1400, generate-questions 700→1200, profile-synthesis 600→1000, business-review 1024→2048, chat 512→900); hardened the portfolio-brief fallback to regex-salvage the `brief` string + drop callouts instead of ever dumping raw JSON; HomeView brief cache key v6→v8 to flush the cached break. (2) **Formatting:** every Pip text surface now renders structured markdown (headline + `##` sections + bullets + bold). `MarkdownText` was already wired into chat, Brief Me, cadence brief, and meeting summaries; added the **daily brief** (HomeView: replaced the `renderBriefWithGlows` splitter with `MarkdownText` + a `makeAccountLinkify` factory so account names stay tappable Glow links *inside* the markdown, including when bold) and the **QBR** (`BusinessReviewModal` plain pre-wrap → `MarkdownText`; prompt switched `•` → `- ` bullets + bold, no glyphs since QBR text is copy-pasted into other tools). Prompts updated: `portfolio-brief.js` structure rule rewritten (was "No headers. No bullets."), `api/pip.js` PIP_FORMATTING gained the glyph vocabulary + a few-shot example; emails explicitly excluded from markdown/glyphs. Test: `src/components/markdownGlyphs.test.js` locks the token-safety property. No schema changes.
- ✅ **Pip model tiering — Sonnet on the surfaces that matter (June 2026)** — Reasoning-heavy, user-facing, low-frequency Pip surfaces moved to Sonnet 4.6: Ask Pip chat (`api/pip.js` chat mode), portfolio question generation (`generate-questions`), daily portfolio brief (`portfolio-brief`), profile synthesis (`profile-synthesis`), QBR (`business-review`). Meeting summarize stays Sonnet. High-volume/mechanical stays Haiku 4.5: per-account Brief Me + cadence brief + email (`api/pip.js` brief/email modes), terminology extraction (`detect-terminology`), state compression (`pip-state-refresh`), leadership readout. Each Sonnet surface reads a per-surface env override (`PIP_CHAT_MODEL`, `PIP_QUESTIONS_MODEL`, `PIP_DAILY_BRIEF_MODEL`, `PIP_PROFILE_MODEL`, `PIP_QBR_MODEL`) so the tier re-dials in Vercel without a redeploy. `_pipUsage.js` cost table already covers Sonnet (3× Haiku). Docs: `ai-governance.md` model-selection rewritten + `product-overview.md` model-tiering note + PDFs.
- ✅ **Pip structured suggestions — "Pip proposes, you approve" (June 2026)** — A drip question carries a structured `suggestion` intent (attached at creation, since the account/contact is known): `contact_role` → `folio_contacts.title`, `account_objective` → `folio_accounts.objective`, `account_system` → `folio_accounts.systems[]`. On answer, a pre-checked "Also save to…" toggle on the HomeView drip card + PipCatchUp applies it via `applyPipSuggestion` (App.jsx) through existing `updateAccount`/`folio_contacts` paths with a confirming toast; untick to keep as a plain fact. Never silent; never touches health/tier. Cross-portfolio surfaces (daily brief, leadership readout) intentionally omit per-account systems as noise. - ✅ **12-item audit bug batch (June 2026)** — Fixed in one commit across 15 files: (1) stuck project detection used `s.done/s.done_at` but stages use `s.completed_at` — every in-progress project was falsely flagged stuck; (2) `update_account_health` Pip tool wrote to dead `status` column instead of `status_override` — voice/chat health commands were silently no-ops; (3) `leadership-readout.js` filtered on `"green"/"yellow"/"red"` but snapshots store `"healthy"/"watching"/"at_risk"` — boss readout always showed zero counts; (4) `allItems` in App.jsx loaded once with no realtime sync — Home and Commitments lagged until page reload; (5) `detectKnowledgeGaps` gated on `onboarding_status === "done"` but `profile-synthesis.js` never returned that value — Phase-2 question drip was permanently dormant; (6) `business-review.js` had no rate limit; (7) 1:1 portfolio brief lacked `overdue_items` array — couldn't name specific overdue items; (8) `pipIntent.js` routed "summarize"/"email" phrases into persona-stripped JSON modes without account context — broken chat replies; (9) `useToneTrend.js` NEGATIVE list contained words that never appear in stored `pip_tone` values — "Cooling ↘" pill never fired correctly; (10) contact assignee in `PipSummarizePreview` used `c.name` as value, landing names in the `assignee_email` column; (11) `callPortfolioBriefPip` and `callBusinessReviewPip` in `pip.js` were missing auth headers — daily brief and QBR silently 401'd on every call; (12) `closeItem` and `useCommitmentNudges.markDone` set only one of `done`/`status` — split-brain between commitment nudge system and item lists.
- ✅ **Gauge project auto-complete (June 2026)** — `ProjectStageEditor.commitStages()` now checks if all stages have `completed_at` set after every toggle. If all done → auto-sets project `status: "complete"`. If any stage un-toggled on a complete project → reverts to `"in_progress"`. Previously projects sat at "in_progress" forever with no indication a manual status update was needed.
- ✅ **Pip daily brief overhaul — 11 items (June 2026)** — Root cause: brief was account-health-centric only; if all 37 accounts computed "healthy," Pip said "quiet morning" even when the AM had overdue tasks, commitments due, and stuck projects. Full fix in three batches:
  - **Workload data** — brief now receives overdue tasks (by name), overdue commitments, commitments due this week, today's cadences, stuck projects (named + account), cold healthy accounts (30+ days no contact), unsummarized draft meetings, account objective for flagged accounts
  - **Tier data** — `tier` now sent per snapshot so `[MAJOR]` prefix can appear in flagged account lines; prompt's "lead with Major" instruction now actually works
  - **Prompt rewrite** — explicit triage order (overdue commitments → fires → Major overdue → stuck/cadences → cold), length-scaling rule (2-3 sentences clean / 5-7 heavy), one-paragraph-break structure rule, "end urgent items with a concrete next action" rule
  - **Callout schema upgrade** — callouts now include `action` (verb phrase), `priority` (now/this_week/watch), `tier`; HomeView chips render priority-colored dot, bold action verb, `[M]` tier badge
  - **Health momentum delta** — `useAccountSnapshots` now fetches 8 days of history; brief computes accounts trending worse (healthy→watching→at_risk) or recovering, surfaces them with directional label
  - **Tone trend** — accounts with 2+ negative/mixed `pip_tone` readings in last 3 days flagged as "COOLING"; warming trend surfaced too
  - **Champions + blockers** — `allContacts` threaded from App.jsx into HomeView; brief includes champion and blocker names per account so Pip can factor relationship power map into next-step recommendations
  - **Cross-account themes** — `useRecentThemes` (already existed, was unused) now wired to brief; themes appearing on 3+ accounts flagged as portfolio signals (e.g. "pricing came up on 4 accounts this month")
  - Cache key bumped to `v6` on final batch so brief regenerates immediately

Pip sets it based on first-person promise language ("I'll get you...", "we'll have X by...", "I'll follow up..."). Pre-flagged rows show a teal "✦ Commitment" toggle in `PipSummarizePreview`; user can un-toggle before applying. `is_commitment` passes through `applyPipPlan` to `folio_tasks`.

- ✅ **Cross-account ⌘K search** — CommandPalette now searches `folio_meetings.notes` and `folio_tasks.title` across all accounts when query is ≥3 chars (debounced 300ms, ilike match). Results appear under "Notes" and "Items" groups with account name + excerpt. Clicking navigates to the account.

SQL: `supabase/folio_items_unification.sql` — **run in production Supabase**.

- ✅ **Pip V2 brain — correction log + read-back + compression + missed_item + routed_account_changed** — `pip_correction_log` table (`correction_type`: summary_edit | rejected_row | item_text_edit | task_text_edit | missed_item | routed_account_changed) with RLS scoped to auth.uid(). `usePipCorrections` hook + `logCorrection(payload)` helper. Capture surfaces: MeetingsTab summary edits (on-blur diff against last-saved Pip output), PipSummarizePreview row rejections + manually-added missed items, TaskDetailPanel + ProjectStageEditor + StandingBoardView + MyQueueView item-text edits (guarded by `pip_created_at` age — only counts within 7 days of Pip creation), account-override moves. Unified `TaskDetailPanel` handles both new-task and edit-from-queue flows with every custom field rendered by type. `StandingBoardView` renders the kanban (one column per `task_status_columns` id) inside the expanded project row. `MyQueueView` flattens tasks across all projects assigned to the current user with Live / Planning / All sub-filters and an optional group-by-project toggle. Project status bubbles into task display via `PLANNING` / `ON HOLD` chips on planned/on_hold projects. "Stages" renamed to "Tasks" everywhere user-facing; DB column name stays `stages` for backwards compat.

## Ripped (deliberate simplification)

Personal Mode focus. Schema stays for future re-build when corporate data integration lands.

- 🪓 **Pipeline V2 + Revenue History + Shop Metrics + revenue surfaces (May 2026)** — the Pipeline nav item, `PipelineView`, Log Month modal, MoM/YoY deltas, sparklines on account cards, MoM trend arrows, revenue display in account card meta + account detail header, Revenue YTD + Revenue Trend + Shop Connections cards on Overview, revenue input on AddAccountModal, Shop Metrics overlay, `useAccountMetrics` hook, financial helpers in `metricsUtils.js` (`displayRevenue`, `fmtRevenue`, `momPct`, `yoyPct`, `momDelta`, `fmtPct`, `fmtDelta`, `latestRecord`, `accountRecords`, `MONTH_NAMES`, `parseRevenueText`), `metricsUtils.test.js`, "revenue" sort option, pipeline mark in Onboarding tour, Pipeline filters from the wishlist, "Revenue/tier/pipeline don't apply" notes in Pip context, revenue/shop secondary-signal sentences in `accountInsights.jsx`, `revenueTrend` + `shopConnections` in PipView context payload. DB columns (`revenue`, `revenue_amount`, `folio_revenue_history`, `folio_shop_metrics`) intact. ShopsTab on MSO accounts stayed (operational child shop list). `pickV` survives in `metricsUtils.js` because it's reused across non-financial insight builders. The `pipeline` glyph in `Mark.jsx` stays in the family. Why: Folios is a notepad-on-steroids / external brain — revenue surfaces showed empty data and made the app feel busy without delivering value. Compliance blocks real revenue ingestion for the foreseeable future; git history is the safety net.

**Security hardening — shipped in code, two items need Supabase dashboard toggle:**

- ✅ Rate limiting on Pip API (20 req/min per user, in-memory)
- ✅ Hardcoded anon key removed — env vars only
- ✅ Audit log SQL written (`supabase/audit_log.sql`) — run when ready
- ✅ Session timeout — 60 min inactivity auto-logout
- ✅ Password strength enforcement — 8 chars, uppercase, number required on signup
- ⚙️ **Email verification** — enable in Supabase Dashboard → Auth → Settings → "Enable email confirmations"
- ⚙️ **2FA (TOTP)** — enable in Supabase Dashboard → Auth → Settings → "Enable MFA"
- 🔜 Active sessions page — UI to view/revoke sessions (not yet built)

## Feature Wishlist / Roadmap

High and medium priority items are now in the **Pending Updates** queue above.

### Cadence (once built)
- [ ] **Cadence analytics** — meeting frequency per account, open item age, account health trends over time, Pip flags accounts untouched in 30+ days. Hold until enough data exists to make it meaningful.
- [ ] **Power BI integration** — connect Supabase directly to Power BI via Postgres connection string for full dashboard reporting. No special integration needed, just expose the DB connection. Hold until data volume justifies it.

### Future / bigger features
- [ ] **Render thrash detector** — Phase 6 observability catches React errors and uncaught exceptions, but it doesn't catch infinite render/refetch loops (the app isn't crashing, just spinning). Example bite: the Activity dropdown strobing because `fromDate` recomputed `Date.now()` every render → filters identity changed → useActivity refetched in a loop. The error boundary never fired. Idea: lightweight render-rate detector at the App level — if a hook's effect fires > N times in M seconds, log a `error_type='render_thrash'` row to `folio_errors` with the suspicious hook name + stack. Surfaces silent perf disasters before users notice the fans spinning. Not v1.
- [ ] **Unified org vocabulary layer** — aliases (item 27), the glossary (`folio_pip_facts`), terminology gap-detection (item 10 Lane C), and account/brand mappings are all the same thing wearing different hats: "what this team calls things." Once each piece is mature, collapse them into one shared org-scoped knowledge base that every Pip surface reads from — one place that holds brands, internal codenames, distributor names, program names, person shorthands, and preferred phrasing. This is what makes the whole app feel like it *knows you*. Don't build until the constituent pieces (27, glossary, 10-Lane-C) have shipped and proven their shape; this is the consolidation pass that unifies them.
- [ ] **Lanyard real auth** — connect Lanyard users to Folios users via Supabase Auth
- [ ] **Lanyard → Folios live sync** — post-conference notes flow into Folios automatically once auth is shared
- [ ] **CRM integrations** — Salesforce / HubSpot sync
- [ ] **Mobile app** — React Native wrapper or PWA improvements
- [ ] **Revenue-impact Update Calendar v3 — Ambitious (supplier webhook / portal / email parser)** — deferred follow-up. The v1 build (manual entry + external_event type) shipped — see Already shipped: Revenue-impact Update Calendar. v3 would add an auto-ingestion lane so supplier-side and customer-internal changes get logged without manual entry. Big lift; revisit when v1 has enough data to prove the value.
